Muziki Wenye Ujumbe: Video Mpya za Muziki Kutoka Tibet ||| Music With A Message: New Music Videos from Tibet
Mradi wa kutafsiri Blogu uitwao High Peaks Pure Earth hivi karibuni umetupia jicho "muziki wenye ujumbe" kwa kutafsiri mashairi ya nyimbo za Tibet kutoka video za Muziki zilizowekwa kwenye mtandao. ||| The blog translation project High Peaks Pure Earth has recently focused on "music with a message"ù by translating the lyrics of Tibetan songs from music videos that have been uploaded onto the internet.

Kizazi kipya kina majaribu yaitwayo uhuru ||| The new generation has a temptation called freedom

Slovakia, Hungaria: Heri ya Mwaka Mpya! ||| Slovakia, Hungary: Happy New Year!

China: Barafu Iliyotengezwa Uchina ||| China: Made-in-China Snow
Jumapili hii iliyopita tarehe 1 Novemba, Beijing ilishuhudia kuanguka kwa mapema zaidi kwa theluji katika miaka 22 iliyopita. ||| This past Sunday on November 1, Beijing saw its earliest snowfall in 22 years.
Badiliko hilo la ghafla la hali ya hewa, lililofunika kabisa mji mzima kwa barafu, liliwashangaza wakazi wengi. ||| The sudden change in weather, which blanketed the entire city in snow, surprised many residents.
Lakini vyombo vya habari viliripoti baadaye kwamba uangukaji huo wa barafu ulisababishwa na ofisi ya kurekebisha hali ya hewa mjini hapo. ||| But the news media later reported that the snowfall had actually been enhanced by the city's weather modification office.
Maelezo nyuma ya mvua hiyo bandia ilikuwa ni kwa sababu Beijing imekuwa ikikabiliana na ukame. ||| The reasoning behind the forced precipitation was because Beijing had been experiencing a drought.
Usiku kabla ya barafu, serikali ililipua angani kemikali ya fedha ya ayodaidi. ||| The night before the snow, the government had fired silver iodide into the sky.
Athari zilizojitokeza ni kuongezeka kwa theluji kwa tani milioni 16. ||| The resulting effect increased the amount of snow by 16 million tons.
"Hatutapoteza fursa yoyote ya kutengeneza mvua bandia kwa kuwa Beijing inakabiliwa na ukame unaotishia,"ù alisema Zhang Qiang, kiongozi wa ofisi ya kurekebisha hali ya hewa, kwa vyombo vya habari vya taifa. ||| "We won't miss any opportunity for artificial precipitation since Beijing is suffering from the lingering drought,'ù said Zhang Qiang, the head of the weather modification office, to the state media.
China ina historia ya kutengeneza mvua kwa kulazimisha, hasa wakati wa kujaribu kusitisha ukame. ||| China has a history of artificially inducing rain, usually in cases to stop drought.
Katika nyakati nyingine, ofisi ya kurekebisha hali ya hewa imepunguza mvua kuhakikisha anga linakuwa tupu, mfano wakati wa gwaride la Siku ya Uhuru au wakai wa michezo ya Olimpiki. ||| At other times, the weather modification office has reduced the rain to ensure clear skies, such as during the National Day parade in October or the 
Beijing Olympic Games.
Wanamtandao wamegawanyika katika mitazamo yao kuhusu barafu hii iliyotengenezwa mwishoni mwa juma lililopita. ||| Netizens have been divided in their opinions about this past weekend's man-made snow.
Wengine waliandika kwa ushabiki kuhusu uzuri wake.||| Some wrote gleefully about its beauty.
Hali ya Hewa ya Beijing ni nzuri kupindukia. ||| Beijing's weather is unimaginably fantastic.
Bila tahadhari, barafu ilianza kudondoka. ||| Without warning, it began to snow.
Na ilikuwa aina ya barafu ambayo isingeweza kusafishwa kiurahisi na kudhibitiwa. ||| And it was the kind of snow that couldn't be easily cleaned up and managed.
Nilisikia kwamba barafu hiyo ilikuwa ya kutengenezwa. ||| I heard that the snow was man-made.
Lakini sijali. ||| But I don't care.
Tunapenda hali ya hewa ya aina hii. ||| We love this kind of weather.
Wengine, hata hivyo, wamekerwa. ||| Some, however, have been more annoyed.
Niliposikia kuwa barafu hiyo ni ya kutengenezwa, ilibidi nishangae ni mtu gani aliyewaza kuwa huu ulikuwa ni wakati sahihi wa barafu kuanguka? ||| After I heard that it was man made, I had to wonder who was the person who thought this was a good time for it to snow?
Kila mahali watu walikutwa bila ya kujiandaa na baridi na matatizo mengine mabaya yanayohusiana na umeme, msongamano na mfumo wa kupasha nyumba joto. ||| Everywhere people have been caught off guard by the cold and the other thorny problems related to power, traffic and heating.
Katika jukwaa la mtandaoni, mtumiaji mmoja alilalamika kwamba seriali ilipaswa kuwatahadharisha watu kabla ya wakati, na kuongeza kwamba safari nyingi za ndege kwenye viwanja vya ndege zilicheleweshwa. ||| On an Internet forum, one user complained that the government should have warned people ahead of time, adding that many of the flights at the airport were delayed.
Kwa mtazamo wangu, aina hii ya moyo wa "mwanadamu kuyashinda maumbile ya asili" ni mzuri, ingawa wakazi wa Beijing "walilazimishiwa" kipindi cha baridi. Kama wanaweza kutatua kweli madhara yaliyotokana na ukame basi kufanya hivi kuna faida. ||| In my view, this type of "man can conquer nature" spirit is good, even though Beijing residents were "winterized."ù If they can really solve the damage wrought by the drought then this has its merits.
Lakini namna kitengo cha hali ya hewa kilivyoshindwa kumjulisha yeyote kabla ya wakati si sahihi kabisa. ||| But the way the weather bureau didn't inform anyone ahead of time isn't quite right.

Mwanablogu alishangazwa kama kuna mtu ana haki ya kubadili hali ya hewa. ||| One blogger wondered if anyone has the right to alter the weather.

Kwa mfano, barafu iliyotokea wakati huu ilikuwa ni kwa sababu Beijing ilikuwa inakabiliwa na ukame. ||| For example, the snowfall that happened this time was because Beijing was suffering from a drought.

Je, hii haitasababisha ukame mkubwa zaidi katika Shandong? ||| Will this cause an even bigger drought in Shandong?

Ukame umeathiri heka 800,000 za mashamba kufikia mwishoni mwa Oktoba, vyanzo rasmi vilikadiria, na tufani ya barafu inasemekana kuwa ilihitajika sana kama msaada kwa wakulima wa sehemu hiyo. ||| The drought has affected 800,000 hectares of farmland by the end of October, official sources estimated, and the snow storm was said to be a much-needed boon to local farmers.
Lakini si wakulima wote katika eneo hilo waliofaidika. ||| But not all farmers in the region benefited.

Kwa uchache hivi ndivyo tulivyoelewa kutokana na taarifa za habari kuhusu jinsi Marekani ilivyopigwa ngeu katika mahusiano yake na nchi hizo ukiiondoa Irani. ||| At least this is what we understood from the news reports about how the States are scared on its relations with these countries excluding Iran.

Ni jambo la kustaajabisha jinsi mbavyo Israel ilijiamini sana katika ushindi wake dhidi ya Hamas! ||| It is amazing how Israel was too confident from its victory on Hamas !

Nilitania leo kwenye Twita ||| I joked today on Twitter
kwamba naamini inawezekana dunia itakabiliana na suala hili katika njia sawa na ile ambayo watu wa kawaida hukabiliana na aibu inayotokea baada ya ngono ya kushtukiza: Kila mmoja alipata uroda sipokuwa kuonana wakiwa uchi na hivi sasa wanataka kumaliza haraka aibu ile na kujidai kuwa hakuna lililotokea.Nimekuwa nikifuatilia tovuti za habari siku nzima ili nione ni kwa jinsi... ||| that I believe the world will probably deal with this the same way regular people deal with post-one-night-stand-hook-up awkwardness: Everyone had their fun but seen each other naked and now they just wanna do their walk of shame and pretend it never happened.I have been monitoring media websites the entire day waiting to see how...

Mwanamuziki mmoja wa Afrika Mashariki awashinda wengine wote kwa umaarufu wa mtandaoni duniani ||| One East African Musician beats all odds for a global fan base
Si wengi wanamfahamu kama Mwanaisha Abdalla bali kama Nyota Ndogo, ni jina linalojulikana kwenye kila nyumba katika Afrika Mashariki. ||| Not many know her as Mwanaisha Abdalla, but Nyota Ndogo, is a household name in East Africa.
Amekuwa akijikusanyia mashabiki wa muziki wa mahadhi ya Afrika Mashariki kwa zaidi ya miaka mine sasa. ||| She has been collecting fans of her eclectic East African sound for over 4 years now.
Blogu yake kwa upande mwingine imekuwa ikifanya kazi kwa miaka mitatu. ||| Her blog, on the other hand, has been running for 3 years.
Hakuna shaka kwamba blogu yake imechangia kukua kwa umarufu wake wa mtandaoni. ||| There is no doubt that the blog has contributed to the growth of her online fan base.
Akiwa amezaliwa mwaka 1981 kwenye Jimbo la pwani la Mombasa, Nyota Ndogo ametokea kwenye historia ya kinyenyekevu. ||| Born in 1981 in the Kenyan Coastal province of Mombasa, Nyota Ndogo has come from a very humble background.
Aliacha shule akiwa na umri mdogo na baada ya muda, akafanya kazi kama mfanyakazi wa ndani mpaka alipogunduliwa na Andrew Burchell kama mtu mwenye kipaji cha kuimba. ||| She dropped out of school at a young age and for quite some time, worked as a house help until she was discovered by Andrew Burchell as a talented singer.
Sasa ana CD tatu zilizotoka kwa jina lake, CHEREKO, NATOKA MBALI NA WEWE na MPENZI. ||| Now she has 3 cd's released under her name, CHEREKO, NATOKA MBALI NA WEWE and MPENZI.
Ameshirikishwa vilevile katika makusanyo matatu ya kimataifa kama WORLD 2003, THE ROUGH GUIDE TO KENYA na OFF THE BEATEN TRACK. ||| She has also featured on 3 international compilations WORLD 2003, THE ROUGH GUIDE TO KENYA and OFF THE BEATEN TRACK.
Pia anashikilia mbili ya Tuzo za muziki za Kisima za Kenya: Mwimbaji bora wa Taraab 2003 na Mwimbaji bora wa kike 2005. ||| She is also holder of two Kenya Kisima Music Awards: Best Taraab Singer 2003 and Best Female Singer 2005.
Nyimbo zake ambazo nyingi ni za Kiswahili zenye maneno machache ya Kiingereza zinaimbwa kwa mahadhi ya Taarab yanayosikika zaidi kwenye ukanda wa mwambao wa Afrika Mashariki na pia Kapuka na Genge, mahadhi ya muziki unaosikika zaidi maeneo ya bara ya Kenya. ||| Her songs, which are mostly in Kiswahili with a few in English, are sang in the Taarab genre heard mostly in the East African Coast as well as in Kapuka and Genge, music genres heard mainly on the Kenyan mainland.
Je ni namna gani mtu mwenye historia kama hiyo anaweza kujifunza kuutumia mtandano wa intaneti kwa faida yake kama Msanii wa Kenya anayechipukia? ||| So how does someone with such a background learn to harness the internet to her advantage as a growing Kenyan based Artist?
Hili ni swali linalokujia kichwani unapotembelea blogu yake. ||| This is the question that comes to mind when you visit her blog.
Humo, anasema kila kitu kinachomhusu yeye kama msanii kwa kutumia mtazamo binafsi ukilinganisha na habari na taarifa za vyombo vya habari zinazohaririwa ambapo mtu anaweza kuzipata kwenye sehemu ya burudani wkenye magazeti na majarida. ||| In it, she shares everything about herself as an artist from a personal perspective as opposed to the edited media stories and information that one will find in the entertainment section of a newspaper or magazine.
Kutoka kwenye video za nyimbo zake mpaka kwenye mashairi ya nyimbo zake mpaka kwenye picha zake zinazomwonyesha akitumbuiza na wasanii wenzake na mashabiki wake, mtu anaweza kujisikia kuunganishwa na kuwekwa karibu zaidi na Nyota Ndogo kwa kupitia blogu yake. ||| From music videos of her songs to lyrics to photos of her performing with fellow artists and fans, one can feel a more intimate connection with Nyota Ndogo through her blog.
Kublogu hakujawa uzoefu rahisi kwake kama alivyokiri kwenye makala yake ya blogu ya tarefhe 27 Julai, 2006 saa 7.43 mchana. ||| Blogging has not been an easy experience for her as she confessed in her blog post on 27th July, 2006 at 1.43 pm.
Almanusura niachane na blogu yake kwa sababu ilikuwa inaniwia vigumu kupata mtundiko mpya. Kumbe ilikuwa ni mimi niliyekuwa natumia kivinjari kisichopatana. ||| wow I'd nearly given up with the blog as it was proving difficult to get a new post up. It turned out to be me using an incompatible browser.
Kwa hiyo nimerejea na kivinjari cha zamani Internet Explorer. ||| So I'm back on good old Internet Explorer.
Kama hii itafanya kazi tegemea picha kadhaa hivi karibuni sababu mengi yametokea. ||| If this works expect some pix up soon so much has happend.
Kwa kuangalia kwenye posti za hivi karibuni kwenye blogu yake, kwa hakika mtu anaweza kuona kuwa Nyota amefahamu vizuri sana kutumia vyenzo za kublogu. ||| Looking at her current blog posts, one can indeed see that Nyota has known quite well how to use the blogging tool.
Hili kwa bahati mbaya sana haliwezi kusemwa kwa Wasanii wengi wengine wa Afrika Mashariki kwa sababu sikuweza kupata blogu yoyote ya msanii mwingine. ||| This unfortunately cannot be said of many other East African Artists, as I could not find any other artist's blog.
Inaonekana, mtu hahitaji kuwa msomi kujua namna ya kublogu, baada ya yote, ni nyenzo tu. ||| It seems, one need not be educated to know how to blog; it is, after all, a tool.
Angalia Moja kwa Moja Yanayojiri Sasa Hivi Katika Mkutano wa Global Voices ||| Watch the Global Voices Summit Live Now!
Mkutano wa Sauti za Dunia wa 2012 umeshafunguliwa muda mfupi uliopita katika jiji la Nairobi, nchini Kenya. ||| The 2012 Global Voices Summit has just opened in Nairobi, Kenya (July 2-3).
Tungetamani sana ungeweza kujumuika nasi pale, lakini kama hilo haliwezekani, waweza pia ukatutazama moja kwa moja kupitia mtandao wa intaneti na pia tukaweza kujadiliana papo kwa hapo. ||| We wish you could be with us there in person, but if you can't you can still watch the livestream and chat with us live.

Lengo la kongamano hili ni kujadili kuhusu upana na umuhimu wa vyombo vya habari za kiraia za mtandaoni ulimwenguni kote. ||| The goal of the Summit is to explore the range and importance of online citizen media around the world.

Udhibiti Nchini Singapore ||| Censorship in Singapore
Katika kipindi cha mwezi hivi, mamlaka za Singapore zimesababisha kelele kubwa baada ya kupiga marufuku filamu ya aliyewahi kuwa mfungwa wa kisiasa na kumkamata mtunzi Mwingereza wa kitabu kilichoandiaka kuhusu adhabu ya kifo nchini humo. ||| In a space of a month, Singapore authorities caused a major uproar when they banned a film of an ex-political prisoner and arrested a British author who wrote a book about the death penalty in Singapore.
Picha hii imechukuliwa kutoka kwa The Online Citizen ||| Picture taken from The Online Citizen
Mnamo Julai 12 mwaka 2010, Mamlaka ya Maendeleo ya Vyombo vya Habari ilitangaza uamuzi wake wa kuipiga marufuku filamu (kuanzia Julai 14, 2010) inayomuonyesha Dr Lim Hock Siew akizungumza hadharani juu ya uzoefu wake wa kuwa kizuizini chini ya Sheria ya Usalama wa Ndani. ||| On 12 July 2010, the Media Development Authority announced its decision to ban a film (starting from 14 July 2010) depicting Dr Lim Hock Siew speaking publicly on his experience being detained under the Internal Security Act.
Filamu ilitengenezwa chini ya uongozi wa Martyn See. ||| The film was filmed by Director Martyn See.
Bw. See alitakiwa kuondoa filamu hiyo kwenye YouTube. ||| Mr See was also asked to remove the film from YouTube.
Unaweza kusoma maelezo ya filamu hiyo hapa. ||| You can read the transcripts of the film here.
Mwanablogu wa Singapore, Lucky Tan ametaka ukweli kusemwa wazi: ||| Singaporean blogger Lucky Tan called for the truth to be told:
Kimsingi kinachosemwa na MICA ni kwamba wameipiga marufuku filamu hiyo kwa kuwa wanataka ukweli pekee ndio usemwe lakini filamu hii imejaa mambo mengi ya uongo, ulaghai na kupindishwa. ||| Basically what MICA is saying is they banned this film because they want only the truth to be told and this film is full of falsehoods, lies and distortions.
Dr Lim Hock Siew alikamatwa na kuwekwa kizuizini kwa miaka 20 bila kifikishwa mahakamani. ||| Dr Lim Hock Siew was detained for 20 years without trial.
Katika kipindi hicho serikali ya PAP ilikuwa na wakati wa kutosha kuonesha ushahidi na kusema ukweli ili kwamba wote tuweze kushuhudia kazi nzuri iliyofanywa na ISD katika kutukinga na maovu. ||| During that period, the PAP govt had all the time to show the evidence and tell the truth so that we can all see how wonderful a job the ISD has done to protect us from evil.
Bado tunangoja. ||| We are all still waiting.
Picha hii imechukuliwa kwa Jacob Geroge ||| Picture taken from Jacob Geroge
Mnamo Julai 18, mwandishi Muingereza Alan Shadrake alikamatwa na polisi wa Singapore akiwa hotelini kwa tuhuma za "jinai ya kuharibu sifa"ù siku moja baada ya kitabu chake cha, Once a Jolly Hangmanù: Haki Kwenye Gati Nchini Singapore, ambacho kilikosoa mfumo wa mahakama wa Singapore kilipozinduliwa. ||| On 18th July, British author Alan Shadrake was arrested by Singapore police in his hotel on charges of "criminal defamation", a day after his book, Once a Jolly Hangman: Singapore Justice in the Dock, which was critical of the Singapore judicial system, was launched.
Kitabu hicho kiliondolewa kwenye maduka makubwa ya vitabu nchini Singapore. ||| His book was also removed from major bookstores in Singapore.
Alishikiliwa kwa siku mbili ambapo Shirika la Haki za Binadamu la Kimataifa Amnesty International na Wanahabari Wasiokuwa na Mipaka walitaka aachiwe. ||| He was detained for two days in which Amnesty International and Reporters Without Borders called for his release.
Blogu ya masuala ya kijamii-na-ya-kisiasa ya Singapore, The Online Citizen ilijiuliza kwa nini Bw. Shadrake alituhumiwa kwa tuhuma hizo za jinai ya kuharibu sifa: ||| Singapore socio-political blog The Online Citizen wondered why Mr Shadrake was charged with criminal defamation:
Kitabu cha Alan Shadrake "Once a Jolly Hangman"ù ni simulizi inayokosesha raha. ||| Alan Shadrake's book "Once a Jolly Hangman"ù makes for uncomfortable reading.
Kitabu hiki kinaweza kuwa kiliwakosesha raha baadhi ya watawala kiasi cha kuwalazimu kumkamata Mr Shadrake kwa kutumia sheria mabayo inatumika kwa nadra sana ya jinai ya kuharibu sifa. ||| The book might have made those in power uncomfortable enough to arrest Mr Shadrake on the rarely-used, draconian charge of criminal defamation.
Blogu ya kiSingapore, Chemical Generation Singapore, iliandika: ||| A Singaporean blog, Chemical Generation Singapore, wrote:
Kwa kumatwa kwa Shadrake, suala zima limekuwa siyo la kuhusu adhabu ya kifo, na badala yake limehusu zaidi juu ya wapi msaada kutoka nje ya nchi unapokoma kuingilia kati. ||| With the arrest of Shadrake, the whole issue is less about the death penalty, and more about where we draw the line on supposed foreign intervention.
Kuwadhibiti wanasiasa wa ndani wanaopokea pesa toka nje ya nchi hilo sina tatizo nalo. ||| Cracking down on local politicians getting foreign money and logistics is fine with me.
Lakini hili la kumdhibiti mgeni wakati wa uzinduzi wa kitabu chake ni sawa na uchokozi wa kitoo kabisa kwa Oliver Fricker, pengine umezidi kipimo katika kitabu changu. ||| But turning the screws on a foreigner in his book launch, although the foreigner is like a taunting Oliver Fricker and asking for it, is a bit too much in my book.
Labda tu kama kuna zaidi ya yale tunayoyaona ||| Unless there is more than meets the eye here
Mwanaharakati wa kisiasa, Chee Siok Chin ameishutumu serikali kuu ya nchi hiyo kwa kuwa na "siri chafu": ||| Political Activist, Chee Siok Chin accused the Government of having "dirty secrets":
Sasa, ni utawala gani wa kiimla utakaotaka siri zake zianikwe hadharani na kijitabu? ||| Now, which authoritarian regime would want to have its "dirty little secrets"ù blown open in a book?
Vile vile hata kwa hotuba Dr. Lim Hock Siew iliyowekwa na Martyn See kwenye Youtube. ||| The same goes for Dr. Lim Hock Siew's speech that was posted by Martyn See on Youtube.
Bila shaka Martyn ilimbidi kukubaliana na matakwa ya MDA ambayo iliamtaka kuiondoa hotuba hiyo. ||| Of course Martyn had to comply with the MDA who required him to take it down.
Hata baada ya yote, Dr. Lim alizungumzia kuhusu kitendo cha ukiukwaji wa sheria kilichofanywa na ISD cha kumuweka kizuizini kwa miaka 19. ||| After all, Dr. Lim spoke about his unlawful 19-year detention without trial by the ISD.
Tena, ni serikari gani kandamizi ambayo itataka ukweli usemwe juu ya jinsi ilivyo kiasi cha kuzuia urushwaji wa video ambayo mtu yoyote anaweza kuipata? ||| Again, which oppressive regime would want to have the truth told about how it entrenches its power blown open in a video clip that can be accessed by all?
Irani: Vuguvugu la Kijani Laupinga Utawala Tena ||| Iran: Green Movement defies regime again
Upande wa upinzani wa Vuguvugu la Kijani nchini Irani mnamo tarehe 4 Novemba mwaka huu (13 ya Abani) uliendesha maandamano makubwa ya mitaani, baada ya kutumia fursa ya maandamano rasmi yaliyoendeshwa siku hiyo ya kuadhimisha kumbukumbu ya miaka 30 ya ukaliaji wa Ubalozi wa Marekani jijini Teherani. ||| Iran's Green Movement opposition organized mass street protests on the 4th of November (13th of Aban), taking advantage of the official rallies being held on the same day to mark the 30th anniversary of the occupation of the US embassy in Tehran.
Maandamano hayo ya upinzani yalikabiliwa na matumizi ya nguvu kupita kiasi ya kuyavunja yaliyofanywa na vikosi vya usalama. ||| The opposition protests were met with a violent crackdown by security forces.
Kama ambavyo sasa imekuwa jambo la kutarajiwa, vyombo vya habari vya kiraia vya Irani vilirekodi "historia" hiyo kupitia simu zao za mkononi. ||| As has come to be expected, Iranian citizen media recorded "history"ù on their mobile phones.
Waandamanaji jijini Teherani walikanyagakanyaga picha ya Kiongozi Mkuu wa Kidini nchini humo, Ayatollah Ali Khamenei, kitendo ambacho wala kisingefikiriwa miezi michache tu iliyopita. ||| Protesters in Tehran trampled on a portrait of the country's Supreme Leader, Ayatollah Ali Khamenei, an act that would have been unimaginable a few months ago.

Suluhisho la Kiradikali la Umaskini Duniani: Ufunguzi wa Mipaka ||| A Radical Solution For Global Poverty: Open Borders
Tarehe 18 Disemba ilikuwa ni siku ya kusherehekea Siku ya Kimataifa ya Wahamiaji. ||| 18 December was the occasion to celebrate International Migrants Day.
Wakati wa mgogoro uliopo wa hali mbaya ya fedha duniani, uhamiaji kutoka nchi zinazoendelea umelaumiwa na vyama kadhaa vya kisiasa kuwa ndiyo chanzo cha ukosefu wa ajira katika nchi hizo. ||| During the current global financial crisis, immigration from developing countries has been blamed by several political parties as the source of unemployment in their countries.
Japokuwa hapajakuwa na utafiti wowote, mpaka sasa, ambao umethibitisha kuwa uhamiaji umekuwa na mchango wowote muhimu katika tatizo la ukosefu wa ajira, imani hii imeendelea kujikita katika fikra za watu wengi. ||| Even though there hasn't been a single study, so far, that has proved that immigration has had in fact a meaningful role in the employment crisis, this belief remains strongly anchored in the minds of many.
Jambo jingine ambalo limelojikita sana katika jamii zilizoendelea: ni ongezeko la kampeni za misaada ya kibinadamu wakati wa kipindi cha sikukuu. ||| Another phenomenon is also strongly anchored in the fabric of many developed societies: the increase in frequency of humanitarian campaigns around the holiday season.
Naam, kila mwisho wa mwaka katika nchi zilizoendelea zaidi, uanweza kuona kampeni ambazo zinahimiza raia wake kutoa michango ya kupigana na umaskini katika nchi za mbali ambazo hazina bahati. ||| Indeed, at every year's end in the more developed countries, one can observe campaigns that encourage their citizens to make donations to fight poverty in distant, less fortunate countries.
Na zaidi ya taswira za umaskini uliokithiri zinazoonekana mara kwa kwa mara wakati wakipindi cha sikukuu (ambazo pia zinaitwa "ùpicha za ngono ya umaskini"ù katika sekta ya maendeleo pale ambapo taswira za watu maskini zinapotumiwa sana na mahirika ya misaada), pia kuna takwimu za kuogopesha: watu bilioni 1.4 wanaishi kwa chini ya dola 1.25 kwa siku. ||| In addition to the recurring images of extreme poverty around the holidays (also referred to as "poverty porn"ù in the development sector whenever pictures of poor people are excessively exploited by charities), there are some worrying statistics: 1.4 billion people live with less than $1.25 a day.
Bila kujali maendeleo yasiyopingika katika nyingi ya nchi za kiAfrika, ukosefu wa usawa wa kijamii bado unaendelea kustua barani Afrika. ||| Despite some undeniable economic progress in many African nations, social inequality is still even more striking on the African continent.
Wanauchumi wanakadiria kuwa 1/3 ya watu maskini duniani watakuwa wanaishi katika bara la Afrika ifikapo mwaka 2015. ||| Economists also project that 1/3 of the poor in the world will reside on the African continent by 2015.
Ni ukweli, kuwa hali ngumu ya uchumi ni moja ya sababu zilizotajwa na milioni 700 duniani ambao wako tayari kuhama kutoka nchi zao za asili. ||| In fact, economic hardship is one of the key factors mentioned by the 700 million people worldwide who are eager to leave their countries of origin.
watu wanaohamahama nchini Morocco ||| Nomads in Morocco
Mara nyingi inaonekana kana kwamba nchi ambazo hazijaendelea kabisa haziwe tu kuepuka laana ya umaskini, bil ya shaka hazina uwezo wa kukabili ukubwa wa majukumu waliyonayo. ||| It often seems that the least developed countries just cannot escape the scourge of poverty, apparently powerless against the magnitude of the task at hand.
Na zaidi ya hivyo, nchi hizo mara nyingi hukumbushwa jinsi zisivyokuwa na uwezo wa kukidhi mahitaji ya watu wao bila ya misaada ya kimataifa. ||| Moreover, these countries are often reminded of their inability to meet the needs of the population without international support.
Japokuwa misaada ya kimataifa ni matokeo ya matatizo ya dharura, hali hii mara nyingi huchukuliwa kama tusi kwa fahari ya utaifa. ||| Although international aid is a consequence of urgent crises, this situation is often felt as a recurring affront to national pride.
Wataalamu kadhaa wanadai hata hivyo, kuwa umaskini uliokithiri hauepukiki. ||| Various experts postulate, however, that extreme poverty isn't inevitable.
Kwa wataalamu wengi wa kiuchumi, suluhisho la kiradikali zaidi la kupunguza umaskini kwa haraka duniani ni, kufungua mipaka kati ya nchi na kuruhusu wafanyakazi kuhamia sehemu ambazo nguvukazi inahitajika zaidi. ||| The most radical solution to drastically reducing global poverty would be, for many economic experts, opening the borders between countries and allowing workers to migrate where labor is most needed.
Maprofesa Marko Bargaric na Lant Pritchett ni wanazuoni wawili wa kwanza kuwasilisha dhana ya "mipaka iliyo wazi"ù kama suluhisho la kupunguza umaskini duniani. ||| Professors Marko Bagaric and Lant Pritchett are two of the first scholars to introduce the concept of "open borders"ù as a solution to reducing global poverty.
Ili kuhitimisha hivyo, Bagaric anaandika: ||| To this effect, Bagaric writes::
Kutuma rasilimali kwenda sehemu maskini kuna tija. ||| Sending resources to impoverished places has merit.
Lakini ni njia ya taratibu na isiyotabirika ya kuboresha ustawi wa watu. ||| But it is a slow and fickle way of enhancing well-being.
Badala yake, tunafuatilia lengo hili kwa kuwezesha uhamiaji wa watu ili kwamba waweze kusafiri kwenda kule ambapo rasilimali zipo. ||| Instead, we directly pursue this aim by freeing up the flow of people so they can travel to where the goods are.
Tatizo la njaa kwa kifupi ni tatizo la usambazaji, na si la upungufu. ||| The starvation crisis is simply one of food distribution, not shortage.
Njia bora zaidi ya kuongeza kasi ya kupunguza umaskini katika Dunia ya Tatu ni kuongeza uhamiaji kelekea (nchi za) Magharibi kwa kiwango kikubwa. ||| The best way to ameliorate Third World poverty is by massively increasing migration to the West.
Wakiachwa watumie mbinu zao wenyewe watu wengi wataishia kwenye njia endelevu za kujikimu, amabzo zitapelekea kwenye mizani butu kati ya rasilimali zilizoko duniani na watu wake. ||| Left to their own devices many people would gravitate to life-sustaining resources, leading to a rough equilibrium between the world's resources and its population.
Lant Pritchett anafafanua dhana hii kwa kina katika kitabu chake: Waache Watu Wake Waje; Kuvunjwa kwa Ukomo wa Sera ya Uhamiaji wa Kimataifa wa Nguvukazi. ||| Lant Pritchett explains this notion in details in his book: Let Their People Come: Breaking the Policy Deadlock on International Labor Mobility.
Ananukuu matokeo ya tafiti inayodai kuwa: ||| He quotes the results of a study claiming that:
Kuondoa vikwazo vya uchumi vilivyobakia duniani kutaongeza Kipato Cha dunia kwa takriban Dola za Kimarekani bilioni 100. ||| Eliminating the planet's remaining trade barriers would increase global Gross Domestic Product by around 100 billion US dollars.
Kuondoa vikwazo vya uhamiaji, tukilinganisha, kutaweza kuongeza maradufu kipato cha dunia: yaani, ongezeko la kipato cha dunia kwa dola za Kimarekani trilioni 60. ||| Eliminating immigration barriers, by comparison, would as much as double world income: that is, increase global GDP by US $60 trillion.
Ongezeko hili la utajiri litagawanywa, lakini watakaonufaika kwa wingi watakuwa ni watu ambao sasa wanaishi katika nchi maskini. ||| This added wealth would be shared, but the overwhelming beneficiaries would be people who now live in poor countries.
Maandamano ya kuunga mkono haki ya wahamiaji kufanya kazi jijini Paris ||| Demonstrations held in favor of the immigrants' right to work in Paris
Benki ya Dunia ilichapisha tafiti kuhusu mchango wa wahamiaji katika uchumi wa nchi zao za asili kwa njia ya utumaji pesa kutoka nje. ||| The World Bank published a study about immigrants' contribution to the economy of their native countries through remittances from abroad.
Tafiti hiyo pia inaonyesha kuwa pesa zinazotumwa kutoka nje kuelekea nchi zinazoendelea zinatarajiwa kuongezeka na kufikia mpaka dola bilioni 351, na kufikia dola bilioni 481 duniani zikijumuishwa nchi zilizoendelea. ||| The study also shows that remittances are expected to reach as high as 351 billion dollars to the developing countries, and 481 billion dollars globally including the high-income countries.
Tafiti hiyo pia inaeleza kuwa: ||| The study also mentions that:
Mtiririko wa pesa zinazotumwa kulekea nne ya sehemu sita zilizowekwa na Benki ya Dunia uliongezeka zaidi ya ulivyotarajiwa: kwa asilimia 11 kuelekea Ulaya ya Mashariki na Asia ya Kati, asilimia 10.1 kuelekea Asia ya Kusini, asilimia 7.7 kuelekea Asia Mashariki na Pasifiki na aslimia 7.4 kuelekea afrika Kusini ya jangwa la Sahara, bila kujali hali ngumu ya uchumi barani Ulaya na katika sehemu nyingine walizofikia wahamiaji wa Kiafrika. ||| Remittance flows to four of the six World Bank-designated developing regions grew faster than expected: by 11 percent to Eastern Europe and Central Asia, 10.1 percent to South Asia, 7.6 percent to East Asia and Pacific and 7.4 percent to Sub-Saharan Africa, despite the difficult economic conditions in Europe and other destinations of African migrants.
Haihitaji kueleza kuwa, nadharia hizi zilizo tofauti na nadharia za kihafidhina zinahojiwa na wataalamu kadhaa pamoja na wanasiasa. ||| Needless to say, these non-orthodox theories are questioned by various experts and politicians.
Frank salter anafafanua kuwa hofu kubwa iko kwenye matatizo yaliyopo kwenye kila jamii yenye tamaduni mbalimbali: ||| Frank Salter explains that the main concerns come from the inherent dysfunctions of every multicultural society:
Uhamiaji usio na kikomo utaharibu maslahi ya taifa (la Australia) kwa namna ambazo zimeandikwa na wanazuoni wa uchumi, soshiolojia na fani zinazohusiana nazo. ||| Unrestricted migration would harm (Australia's) national interests in ways documented by scholars in economics, sociology and related disciplines.
Madhara makubwa yanatabiriwa kutokea kwenye kile kinachojulikana kuhusu matatizo yaliyopo kwenye utofauti. ||| Much of the harm is predictable from what is known about the dysfunctions of diversity.
Yanayojumuisha ongezeko la ukosefu wa usawa hasa kwenye namna ya ubaguzi wa matabaka yanayotokana na asili za watu. Utofauti pia umehusishwa na kupungua kwa demokrasia, kuzorota kwa uchumi, kuporomoka kwa mshikamano wa kijamii na misaada kutoka nje, vile vile ongezeko la ufisadi pamoja hatari ya migogoro ya kiraia ||| They include growing inequality in the especially invidious form of ethnic stratification. Diversity has also been associated with reduced democracy, slowed economic growth, falling social cohesion and foreign aid, as well as rising corruption and risk of civil conflict
Kutokea kwenye mtazamo wa kisiasa, bara la Ulaya lipo mbali na kufungua mipaka, na pengine ni tofauti ya hivyo. ||| From a political point of view, Europe is far from opening the borders, rather the contrary.
Nchini Ufaransa Sheria ya Gueant inazuia uwezekano wa wahitimu wa masomo kutoka nje kuajiriwa, jambo ambalo limezua miitiko mablimbali. ||| In France, the GuÈant Act restricts foreign graduates' possibility of recruitment, giving birth to various reactions.
Julie Owono, mshirika wa Global Voices, anaelezea maana ya sheria hii na miitiko ya wanablogu mbalimbali wa kiAfrika ambao wanaiona sharia hii kama sababu ya ziada ya kuchangia maendeleo kwenye nchi zao. ||| Julie Owono, Global Voices member, describes the implications of this law and the reactions of various African bloggers that see this law as an additional reason to contribute to the development of their countries.
Katika blogu ya Rue69, Owono anaongezakwamba Sheria ya Gueant pia inawabagua wanafunzi kutoka nje ambao wana uwezo mdogo wa kifedha.. ||| On the Rue69's blog, Owono adds that the GuÈant Act also ostracizes financially limited foreign students.
Barani Afrika, ni wataalamu wachache tu ambao wameisoma dhana ya mipaka iliyo wazi, dhana ambayo, bila ya shaka, iko mbali sana na ukweli uliopo barani ili kuendelezwa. ||| In Africa, only a few experts have studied the concept of open borders, an idea that is, without doubt, too distant from the continent realities to persist.
Profesa wa falsafa wa Chuo Kikuu cha McGill, Arash abizadeh, hataki kuhimiza kufunguliwa kwa mipaka, hata hivyo nasema kuwa mfumo uliopo wa mipaka hauwezi kuhalalishwa kwa mantiki ya uwazi ya kiliberali. ||| McGill University philosophy professor, Arash Abizadeh, doesn't encourage the opening of borders, yet states that the current border system can't be justified by a liberal egalitarian logic.
Abidazeh anasema kuwa ikiwa tunataka kushikilia imani kuwa "binadamu wote wanazaliwa wakiwa huru na sawa"ù, mfumo wa mipaka, wenyewe, ni uvunjifu wa kanuni hiyo. ||| Abidazeh states that if we want to stick to the belief that "All men are born free and equal"ù, the constitution of borders is by itself a violation of such a principle.
Mwanablogu wa kiMalagasi Sly anaandika kuhusu hatari za kufungua mipaka: ||| Malagasy blogger Sly writes about the risks of opening the borders: Mimi ni muAfrika na wakati inaonekana kana kwamba wazo hili litakuwa zuri kuna madhara kadhaa: ||| I'm African and while it seems that this would be a good idea there are some drawbacks
biashara ya watoto ||| child trafficiking
biashara ya mihadarati ||| drug trafficking
Kusambaa kwa VVU na magonjwa mengine ||| spread of HIV and other diseases.
wakimbizi wataunda kambi kwenye nchi tajiri zaidi na kusababisha matatizo ||| refugees will form camps in more prosperous nations causing some problems.
Pamoja na kusema hivyo baadhi ya nchi barani Afrika zina mipaka iliyo wazi na baadhi ya majirani zao. ||| Having said this, some countries in Africa do have open borders with some neighbouring countries.
Sly anagusia ukweli kuwa kufungua mipaka kati ya Kenya, Uganda na Ethiopia, katika jaribio la kuongeza mshikamano wa kiuchumi, ulizua changamoto kubwa katika kanda hiyo wakati wa balaa la njaa la hivi karibuni. ||| Sly refers to the fact that opening the borders between Kenya, Uganda and Ethiopia, in an attempt to increase regional economic integration, raised some major challenges in the region during the recent food crisis.
Dhana hii ya kutumia kufungua mipaka ili kupunguza ukosefu wa usawa kijamii duniani inamaanisha kwamba kupunguza umaskini duniani kungekuwa ndiyo kipaumbele cha juu zaidi duniani. ||| This concept of using open borders to reduce global social inequalities implies that reducing global poverty would be the highest priority in the world.
Kingekuja kabla ya masuala mengine muhimu kama vile usalama wa taifa na maslahi ya taifa ya nchi yoyote. ||| It would come before other important considerations such as national security and the national interests of each country.
Nadharia hii ya Pritchett na Magric bila ya shaka ina upande tata ambao una nia ya kuchokoza mdahalo. ||| This theory of Pritchett and Magric's certainly has a contentious side that aims to provoke a debate.
Hata hivyo, mbali ya madai ya jumuiya ya kimataifa inayotaka kupunguza umaskini duniani, suluhisho la mipaka iliyo wazi linaweza tu kufikiriwa katika muktadha wa namna zake na hauwezi kupewa kipaumbele juu ya vipengele vingine kwenye ajenda ya kimataifa. ||| However, despite the claims of the international community that wants to reduce poverty worldwide, the open-borders solution is only to be considered in specific contexts and won't take precedence over other items on the international agenda.

Venezuela: Wahindi wa Yukpa, Chavez na Mgogoro wa Ardhi ||| Venezuela: Yukpa Indians, Ch·vez and land disputes
Picha za video zinatumwa kwenye mtandao wa intaneti na vyombo vya habari vya kiraia zikionyesha yale yanayojiri kuhusu mgogoro unaoibuka nchini Venezuela kati ya Wahindi wa jamii ya Yukpa wanaoishi katika milima ya Perij·, wamiliki wa ardhi na Rais Ch·vez. ||| Citizen media videos have been uploaded informing of the situation arising in Venezuela between the Yukpa Indians of the Perij· Mountains, landowners and President Ch·vez.
Mgogoro huu kuhusu mipaka ya ardhi umekuwapo kwa takribani miaka 30, yaani tangu pale vikosi vya jeshi vilipowandoa kwa nguvu wanajamii wenyeji ya Ki-Yukpa na kuwapa ardhi hiyo wamiliki wapya walioanzisha mashamba makubwa ya mifugo, hasa ng'ombe, ambao wameendelea kuitumia ardhi hiyo tangu wakati huo. ||| This dispute over land limits is 30 years in the making, when military forces displaced the Indigenous communities of the Yukpa by force and established landowners who have cattle ranches and have been working the lands ever since.
Wahindi wa ki-Yukpa wamejaribu mara kadhaa bila mafanikio kuitwaa upya ardhi waliyoporwa, na hata Rais wa Venezuela, Hugo Ch·vez, alipata kutangaza miaka 10 iliyopita kwamba tatizo hilo la ardhi limalizwe, lakini mpaka sasa hakuna cha maana kilichofanywa ili kupata suluhisho la kubadili hali ya mambo. ||| The Yukpa Indians have attempted to reclaim the lands taken from them, and even the Venezuelan president Hugo Ch·vez declared 10 years ago that the problems with land ownership in the Perij· Mountains should be resolved, but nothing was done to advance solutions.
Kwa sasa Wahindi wa ki-Yukpa wameyatwaa tena mashamba hayo makubwa, na wale wamiliki waliokuwa wakiyashikilia na ambao walitegemea nyama na uzalishaji wa mazao ya mifugo kuendesha maisha wanashindwa kuendelea na kazi zao. ||| Currently the Yukpa Indians have taken over the ranches, and the landowners who live off meat and dairy production are unable to continue their work.
Hali imezidi kuwa tata kutokana na uwepo wa vikosi vya jeshi katika eneo hilo na kulitenga eneo hilo na maeneo mengine ya nchi, hali ni mbaya kiasi kwamba makundi ya Wenyeji hawawezi kutembea kwa uhuru katika ardhi yao na wakati huohuo waandishi wa habari wanazuiwa kuingia ili kuripoti kuhusu vitendo vya uvunjaji wa Haki za Binadamu, hasa vile vinavyosemekana kufanywa na wauaji wa kukodi wa Kikolumbia ambao wamekuwa wakilenga kila mtu; hivi karibuni tu walimshambulia mpaka kumuua kikongwe wa miaka 109 mwenyeji wa eneo hilo. ||| This situation has been made more difficult due to military presence in the area which has caused a siege state, where the Indigenous groups are not allowed to walk freely on their lands or out of them and journalists are blocked from going inside the area to report on human rights abuses such as the alleged hiring of Colombian hit-men who have been targeting entire communities and who beat a 109-year-old indigenous elder to death.
Pamoja na vikwazo vyote hatimaye WaYukpa walifaulu kujipenyeza katika vikwazo vyote vya kuwasiliana na kuifikia jumuiya ya Machique mnamo tarehe 26 Agosti 2008, na hapo Hugo Ch·vez ametangaza kwamba ardhi hiyo haina budi kurejeshwa na kwamba haki za wenyeji wa eneo hilo hazina budi kuheshimiwa. ||| Finally the Yukpa broke through the communication blocks, have gotten through to the media and have reached the community of Machique on August 26th 2008, and Hugo Ch·vez has declared that these lands should be given back and the indigenous community's rights should be respected.
Kwa kupitia blogu ya jamii ya Sauti zenye Kuashiria Haraka, wanaibua maswali mengi kuhusiana na hatma ya mgogoro huu na suluhisho lake: ||| In the collective blog Voces Urgentes, they pose several questions regarding the future of this situation and its resolution:
Hivi, kwa nini kuzuiwa huku kwa wenyeji kumevunjiliwa mbali sasa baada ya Ch·vez kutoa amri? ||| So now, why is the blockage only broken when Ch·vez has spoken?
Nini kilikuwa kikizuia taarifa za kinachoendelea kumfikia Ch·vez? ||| What happened to clue Chavez into what was happening?
Je, mamlaka zimekuwa zikijibu vipi madai yasiyonyamazishika ya Wahindi wa Ki-Yukpa? ||| What have been the actions of the authorities when faced with the constant demands of the Yukpa Indians?
Hivi kwa nini Waziri wa Mambo ya Wenyeji wa Serikali ya Watu, Nicia Maldonado, anatoa matamshi ya kuwataka Wa-Yukpa kuheshimu mali za watu binafsi na kuwataka kuishi kwa kutegemea utalii katika eneo lililojitenga na lililo kame? ||| Why is the Popular Power for Indigenous Affairs minister, Nicia Maldonado, recommending that the Yukpa should respect private property and live of tourism in an isolated and arid area?
Je, ni nani na kwa vigezo vipi ambapo utengwaji wa maeneo ya wenyeji utafanyika? ||| By whom and with which criteria will the demarcation of indigenous lands take place?
Picha ya video iliyopandishwa mtandaoni ni moja tu kati ya dazeni kadhaa zilizopo zinazoonyesha mateso ya jamii hii na kadiri mateso haya yanavyoanza kufahamika kwa umma mpana zaidi. ||| The following online video is only one of dozens documenting the plight of this community and how it is just becoming known to the general public.
Katika picha hiyo, wanajamii hii wanasimulia jinsi mmiliki mmoja wa ardhi alivyojigamba kwao kwamba alikuwa na uwezo wa kufanya chochote kwa sababu tayari viongozi walikwishapokea hongo kutoka kwake, na kwamba kamwe asingetupwa jela hata kama wangekwenda kwa Rais kwa sababu yeye anazo fedha za kutoa ili aachiwe huru: ||| In the video, they relate how one of the landowners told them that he could basically do what he wanted since every authority had been bribed already, and that he wasn't going to go to jail even if he went up to the President himself, because he had money to pay to get out.
Picha nyingine ya video inaonyesha jinsi msafara wa watoa misaada ya kibinadamu walioongozwa na taasisi ya ANMCLA walivyokuwa wakijaribu kupita katika eneo la Wa-Yukpa ili kupeleka misaada ya chakula na dawa kwa wenyeji wa eneo hilo, lakini walizuiwa kupita na maafisa wa kijeshi. ||| This other video shows a humanitarian caravan led by the ANMCLA organization trying to pass into Yukpa territory to deliver food and medication to the indigenous community, but they are blocked by military officers.
Pamoja na hayo, kikosi hichohicho kilichowazuia watoa misaada ya kibinadamu kupita kilikuwa tayari kuruhusu kwa moyo radhi kabisa lori lililobeba chakula cha kulishia nguruwe kupita. ||| Nevertheless, the same army that didnít allow them to pass was perfectly willing to let a truck loaded with food for pigs to pass.
Asasi za kiraia zilifaulu kumshawishi dereva wa lori hilo ëkuonaí kwamba haikuwa haki na ilikuwa kinyume cha katiba kupeleka chakula kwa wanyama wakati ambapo chakula kilichokuwa kipelekwe kwa binadamu kilizuiwa; dereva huyu anaonekana kuelewa kwani alirudisha lori nyuma mpaka mahali kikosi cha jeshi kilipokuwa kimeweka kizuizi. ||| The community organizations managed to convince the truck driver that it was unfair and unconstitutional to deliver food to animals when food for humans wasn't being let through, and he is shown to take the truck back from the picket line.
Katika picha hiyo hiyo ya video, wanaonyeshwa baadhi ya Wa-Yukpa wakiwasili katika mpaka kulipowekwa kizuizi na kueleza kwamba jeshi halina haki ya kutawala jamii za wenyeji, na kwamba jamii hizo hazina budi kuongozwa na viongozi waliochaguliwa na watu, na kwamba watu wana haki ya kukaribisha yeyote wanayemtaka kuingia katika eneo lao. ||| Later in the video, the members of the Yukpa arrive at the border of the siege area and state that no army should control indigenous communities, but that they should be led by community leaders chosen by them, and they should be able to invite people into their territories.
Pamoja na juhudi zote hizo, msafara wa watoa misaada ya kibinadamu hawakuruhusiwa kupita ili kupeleka msaada wa chakula na dawa kwa sababu kikosi cha jeshi kiling'ang'ania msimamo wake, baadhi ya watoa misaada walijeruhiwa, na watatu kati yao walikamatwa. ||| However, the humanitarian caravan wasn't allowed to pass and deliver the food and medicines due to the army's intransigence on this point; several of them were injured, and 3 were arrested.
Siku mbili baadaye, Rais alitambua haki ya Wahindi wa Ki-Yukpa kujitawala na kurejesha ardhi yao mikononi mwao. ||| Two days later, the president recognized the Yukpa Indian's rights to reclaim their lands.

Misri: Picha Zinapoongea Zaidi Ya Maneno ||| Egypt: When Pictures Speak Louder than Words
Makala hii ni sehemu ya ukurasa wetu maalum wa Maandamano ya Upinzani 
Nchini Misri 2011. ||| This post is part of our special coverage of Egypt Protests 2011.
Kadri ya watu milioni tayari wapo kwenye viwanja vya (Ukombozi) vya 
Tahrir jijini Cairo wakiimba, na kumtaka Mubarak aondoke. ||| Up to a million people are already chanting in Tahrir (Liberation) Square, Cairo, calling on Mubarak to leave.
Maandamano ya kumpinga Mubarak yamekuwa yakifanywa nchini Misri kwa siku 11 mfululizo na siku ya leo imepewa jina la Ijumaa ya Kuondoka au Ijumaa ya Mwisho. ||| Anti-Mubarak protests have been held across Egypt for the 11th day in a row and today's is being dubbed as the Departure or Final Friday.

Guinea: Jaribio la Kumuua Kiongozi wa Kijeshi Dadis Camara ||| Guinea: Attempt on Military Leader Dadis Camara's Life
Dadis Camara, ofisa wa jeshi wa Guinea aliyetwaa madaraka mwezi Disemba mwaka jana katika mapinduzi ya kijeshi, alipigwa risasi na mmoja wa wasaidizi wake jana na amesafirishwa kwenda Morocco. ||| Dadis Camara, a Guinean military officer who seized power last December in a coup, was shot yesterday by one of his aides and has been evacuated to Morocco.
Kwa mujibu wa vyanzo kadhaa vya habari, Kapteni Dadis Camara, kiongozi wa kikundi cha jeshi kilitwaa madaraka nchini Guinea mwezi Disemba 2008, alipigwa risasi na kujeruhiwa na mmoja wa wasaidizi wake jana mjini Conakry. ||| According to several news sources, Captain Dadis Camara, leader of the military junta which seized power in Guinea in December 2008, was shot and wounded by one of his aides yesterday in Conakry.
Kiongozi wa serikali isiyo rasmi wa Guinea, aliyetengwa na jumuiya ya kimataifa tangu kuuwawa na kubakwa kwa waandamanaji wa upinzani kulikofanywa na maaskari tarehe 28 Septemba, alisafirishwa kwa ndege kwanda nchini Morocco, ambako aliwasili katika majira ya saa 9 Alasiri GMT. ||| The leader of the de facto government of Guinea, shunned by the international community since the September 28th killing and rape of opposition protesters by soldiers, was flown to Morocco, where he arrived at around 3 P.M. GMT.
Meja KÈlÈtigui Camara, Katibu Mkuu wa ofisi ya Rais, alisema katika mahojiano ya simu kuwa watu wawili amboo hafahamu majina yao, waliuwawa. ||| Major KÈlÈtigui Camara, General Secretary of the Presidency, said in a phone interview that two people, whose names he did not know, were killed.
Wanachama wengine wa kundi hilo la mapinduzi ya kijeshi pia walisafirishwa kwenda Morocco. ||| Two other junta members were also evacuated to Morocco.
Kwenye eneo husika mjini Conakry, hali inaonekana kuwa ya ukimya, kwa mujibu wa vyanzo mbalimbali pamoja simu zilizopigwa kwa magazeti na serikali na mwandishi huyu. ||| On the spot in Conakry, the situation seems to be quiet, according to several sources as well as phone calls made by this author to newspapers and the government.
Hata hivyo, hakuna anayefahamu ukubwa wa majeraha ya kiongozi huyo wa mapinduzi ya kijeshi. ||| However, no one has a clue about the seriousness of the junta leader's wounds.
Mtu mmoja kutoka katika shirika la kimataifa aliniambia kuwa Camara anaweza kuwa alijeruhiwa kichwani au shingoni. ||| Someone from an international organization told me Captain Camara might be wounded in the head or neck.
Maoni ya mwanzo kufuatia habari hii kwenye tovuti ya RFI yameonyesha mitazamo mbalimbali. ||| Some preliminary reactions to the news on the RFI website showed a range of opinion.
Msomaji mmoja aliyeandika bila kutaja jina aliandika: ||| One anonymous reader writes:
Haiwezi kuaminika, haikubaliki, na haiwezi kuhalalishwa kwa ofisa wa cheo cha chini kupiga risasi mkubwa wake. ||| It is unbelievable, unacceptable, and unjustifiable that a junior officer would fire upon his superior.
Afisa huyu mdogo ni lazima akabiliane na matokeo ya vitendo vyake. ||| This junior officer must face the consequences of his actions.
Ninaelewa kwa nini Kapteni Moussa Dadis Camara amesema kuwa jeshi halidhibitiki. ||| I understand why Captain Moussa Dadis Camara has said that the army is uncontrollable.
Hata hivyo, wasomaji wengi, wanaomhusisha Camara uwajibikaji kwa mauaji ya kinyama ya waandamanaji wa upinzani ya tarehe Septemba 28, wanaonekana kuwa wanaamini jaribio la kumuua ni la haki. ||| However, most readers, holding Camara responsible for the September 28th massacre of opposition protesters, seemed to believe the assassination attempt was justice.
Dadis ni mfano hai wa wa matokeo ya kuwasaliti watu wa Guinea. ||| Dadis is living the results of his betrayal of the Guinean people.
Ujasiri kwa watu wa Guinea na hasa wafanyakazi. ||| Courage to the people of Guinea and especially the working people.
Kinachotokea nchini Guinea ni cha kusikitisha; maisha yamepoteza utukufu wake. ||| What's happening in Guinea is really sad; life has lost its sanctity.
Kama jana, raia waliuwawa (28 Septemba), na leo, ni zamu ya mkuu wa kundi la mapinduzi ya kijeshi nchini Guinea. ||| If yesterday, civilians are massacred (the 28th of Septemer), then today, it's the head of the Guinean junta's turn.
Ni onyesho la kusikitisha liliojeÖ ||| What a depressing spectacle.
Kwa kuwa mimi ni Mkongo (DRC), ninajaribu kuiangalia hali hii kama vile ile ya 2001, na kutumaini kuwa watu wa Guinea watanyanyuka kama mtu mmoja na kukomesha mgogoro huu wa kijinga na wenye kutia aibu. ||| Being Congolese (DRC), I try to see this situation like the one in 2001, hoping that the Guinean people will rise as one to put an end to this, such an ignoble and stupid crisis.
Dunia inaihitaji ushiriki wa Guinea katika jumuiya ya kimataifa. ||| The world needs the participation of Guinea in the community of nations.
Jipeni moyoÖ ||| Have courageÖ
Mpaka hapo tutakapota ushahidi unaopinga, ni yeye na ani yeye peke yakeanayewajibika kwa mauaji kwenye uwanja wa taifa tarehe 28 Septemba, katika jina la nguvu. ||| Until proof to the contrary, he and he alone is responsible for the killings in the stadium on September 28th, in the name of power.
Na kama akipata risasi chache kichwani katika jina la nguvu hiyo hiyo kutoka kwa mtu aliye mkono wake wa kuume, basi anastahili kusikia uchungu wa akina mama aliojeruhiwa na kubakwa na majeshi yake. ||| And if gets a few bullets to the head in the name of that same power by his own right-hand man, then he deserves to feel the pain of the women injured and raped by his troops.
Kama dhahama imemuangikia Dadis leo, ninaweza kusema ni kisasi cha watu wa Guinea. ||| If a tragedy has befallen Dadis today, I'd say itís the vengeance of the Guinean population.
Guinea inataka rais ambaye atawawakilisha kila mahali, sio rais ambaye anawatenga na dunia, ambaye anatawala kwa mabavu. ||| Guinea wants a president that can represent them everywhere, not a president who cuts them off from the rest of the world, who rules with tyranny.

Azerbaijan: Bikra ||| Azerbaijan: Virginity

Misri: Watu 10 Wenye Ushawishi Zaidi Nchini ||| Egypt: The top 10 most influential people
Mwanablogu Ahmed Shokeir aliendesha taftishi ya kutafuta watu 10 wenye ushawishi zaidi nchini Misri baada ya kushangazwa na matokeo ya Gamal Mubarak, mtoto wa Rais Hosni Mubarak wa Misri kama mmoja wa washindi 100 wa mwisho wa mwaka 2009 wa TIME. ||| Blogger Ahmed Shokeir conducted a survey to find out the 10 most influential people in Egypt after he was surprised to find out that Gamal Mubarak, son of Egyptian president Hosni Mubarak was among the 2009 TIME 100 Finalists.
Shokeir anaandika: ||| Shokeir writes:
Jambo la kushangaza sana lilikuwa kwamba Mwarabu wa pili mwenye ushawishi zaidi baada ya Shehe Ahmed bin Zayed Al Nahyan, ambaye ni mkurugenzi wa Abu Dhabi Investment Authority, aliyeshika nafasi ya 13 baada ya kupata kura 839,000. ||| The real surprise was the second Arab influential person after Sheikh Ahmed bin Zayed Al Nahyan, Abu Dhabi Investment Authority managing director who was ranked as number 13 with more than 839 thousand votes.
Kwa mara ya kwanza jina la Gamal Mubarak limejitokeza katika nafasi ya 18 ya orodha baada ya kupata kiasi cha kura 832,593. ||| For the first time Gamal Mubarak's name shows up on the Time list in the 18th position with a slight difference, 832,593 votes.
Gamal Mubarak alimshinda Britney Spears (aliyeshika nafasi ya 30) na Barack Obama (nafasi ya 37). ||| Gamal Mubarak preceded Britney Spears (30th) and Barack Obama (37th).

Kwanza kabisa huwa hatuna aina hii ya ushindanishaji nchini Misri mara kwa mara, pili huna budi kutambua kwamba jambo hili liliendeshwa kwenye blogu ya nchini Misri, washiriki wanaweza kusemwa kwamba ilikuwa ni sampuli ndogo sana katika jamii ya Wa-Misri ìZaidi ya washiriki 120 kwenye blogu yake na zaidi ya washiriki 300 kwenye tukio katika face bookî na kwa hiyo baadhi ya watu huenda watasema kwamba sampuli haikuwa wakilishi vya kutosha, hata hivyo, kwa namna ya kushangaza kabisa, baadhi ya majibu yanawakilisha maoni ya Wa-Misri walio wengi. ||| First of all we do not have these kinds of lists in Egypt regularly, second you must know that this was held on an Egyptian blog, the participants are considered a very small sample from the Egyptian society ìMore than 120 participants on his blog and more than 300 participants in the event on the face bookî and some may considered it as unrepresentative sample still most of the answers surprisingly represent the views of most Egyptian people as I see it.
Akitunza kile kizuri ili kukitoa mwishoni kabisa, Zeinobia alianza na washindi bora 9: ||| Saving the best for last, Zeinobia shared the top 9:
Katika nafasi ya 10 yenye pointi 168 yupo kocha wa timu ya taifa ya soka ya Misri Hassan Shahata. ||| In 10th place for 168 points the Egyptian National football team trainer Hassan Shahata.

Katika nafasi ya 5 yenye pointi 215 ni mwanasayansi Ahmed Zowail. ||| In 5th place for 215 points scientist Ahmed Zowail.

Katika nafasi ya 2 yenye pointi 364 ni Gamal Mubarak. ||| In 2nd place for 364 points Gamal Mubarak.
Sasa kuhusu mtu mwenye ushawishi zaidi nchini Misri, ||| As for Egypt's most influential figure,
Na kwa mshangao wangu mkubwa: ||| Now to my surprise:

Zeinobia anatambua kwamba: ||| Zeinobia is aware that:
Taftishi hii ilikuja katika kilele cha matukio ya Khalid hasa kwa umaarufu wake kutokana na vipindi vyake vya TV vya wakati wa Ramadhani, hivyo hicho kilichangia sana matokeo hayo na bila shaka nafasi ya dini katika maisha yetu. ||| This survey came at the seasonal peak of Khalidís popularity after his Ramadan TV shows this year contributed much to this result besides of course the role of religion in our lives.
Hata hivyo, bado anajiuliza kama kweli alistahili kushika nafsi ya kwanza kwenye orodha hiyo. ||| But she still wonders if he deserves to come first in the list.
Ujauzito na Magereza: Afya na Haki za Wanawake Magerezani ||| Pregnancy and Prisons: Women's Health and Rights Behind Bars
Je, wanawake wote wajawazito wanastahili haki sawa za binadamu, au wanawake wajawazito walio jela huziacha haki hizo? ||| Do all pregnant women deserve equal human rights, or do pregnant women in prison forfeit those rights?
Kuna maswali machache yanayokuja akilini kuhusu haki ya mwanamke mjamzito kuishi na kumlea mwanae anapokuwa kapatikana na hatia kwa kosa la jinai la namna fulani: ||| There are a few questions that come to mind regarding a pregnant woman's right to live and to raise her child when she has been convicted for some sort of crime:
Inakuwaje kwao wanapokuwa wajawazito na kupata mtoto wakiwa gerezani? ||| What is it like for them to be pregnant and have their child behind bars?
Je, wanapaswa kuwa kipaumbele wakati kuna wanawake wengine nje ya vyuo vya mafunzo bila msaada wa kitabibu? ||| Should they be a priority when there are other women outside of correctional facilities without medical assistance?
Je, ujauzito unapaswa kuwa juu ya hali nyinginezo za kisheria kumhakikishia mwanamke mjamzito haki zake za kibinadamu? ||| Should maternity overrule any other legal conditions to ensure a pregnant woman's human rights?
Marekani: wanawake walio kwenye uchungu wa kuzaa hawatafungwa tena minyororo. ||| USA: women in labor no longer to be shackled.
Je unaweza kufikira mwanamke akijifungua huku mikono yake ikiwa kwenye pingu na miguu yake ikiwa imefungwa na minyororo kwenye kitanda? ||| Could you imagine a woman giving childbirth with her hands in handcuffs and her feet shackled to the bedposts?
Malika Saada Saar, mwanzilishi na Mkurugenzi Mtendaji wa Mradi wa Rabecca kwa Haki za Binadamu, anatuelezea kuhusu kitendo hiki ambacho bado kinatokea nchini Marekani, ambapo wanawake wajazito wanaotumikia kifungo wamekuwa wakifungwa minyororo wakati wa uchungu na kujifungua na kuwa hiki ni kitendo kilichozoeleka katika baadhi ya magereza (ya kurekebishia tabia), ingawa ni hatari kwa afya ya mama na mtoto. ||| Malika Saada Saar, founder and executive director of the Rebecca Project for Human Rights, tells us about this practice which still happens in the United States of America, where pregnant women serving time have been routinely shackled during labor and childbirth as a common practice in some correctional facilities, even though it is dangerous for the health of both mother and child.
Ifuatayo ni video ya mahojiano yaliyoambatanishwa kwenye makala iliyoandikwa kwa ajili ya mradi wa RH Reality Check, jamii ya mtandaoni kuhusu afya na haki ya uzazi na jinsia inatupa taarifa na uchambuzi kwa afya ya uzazi: ||| The following is a video interview included in the same article written for RH Reality Check, an online community on sexual and reproductive health and rights which does information and analysis for reproductive health:
Kitu gani hutokea kwa mtoto mchanga wa wa mfungwa baada ya kuzaliwa? ||| What happens to an inmate's baby after childbirth?
Nchi mbalimbali zina kanuni tofauti kuhusiana na watoto magerezani. ||| Different countries have different regulations regarding children in prisons.
Kwa mfano, nchini Argentina, kwa mujibu wa Ajintem, chombo cha mawasiliano cha taarifa za uhamamiaji, sheria ilipitishwa mwaka uliopita ikifafanua kwamba wanawake wajawazito, wanawake wenye watoto wadogo chini ya miaka mitano na wale wenye watoto walemavu wangenufaika na mpango wa kutumikia kifungo chao makwao chini ya ulinzi wa nyumbani. ||| For example, in Argentina, according to Ajintem, an information portal for migration information, a law was passed last year specifying that pregnant women, women with children younger than 5 and those with handicapped children would benefit from spending their prison term at home under house arrest.
Sheria hii ingewanufaisha si tu akina mama, ambao kwa kuwa gerezani wasingepata huduma za afya wakati wa ujauzito, lakini pia mtoto, ambaye angelelewa ama katika mazingira yasiyo salama yanayokosa uhuru na upungufu wa udhibiti wa afya na chakula, au wangelelewa mbali na mama, na hivyo kusababisha mlolongo wa matatizo mengine. ||| This law would benefit not only the mother, who in prison wouldn't receive suitable health care during her pregnancy, but also the child, who would either be raised in an unsafe environment deprived of freedom with deficient health controls and food, or be raised away from the mother, causing another series of problems.
Hata hivyo, ujumbe ni kwa ajili ya mahakimu kufuatilia kiini cha sheria na kutoa ruhusa hii kwa wanawake wale ambao hawahusishwi na mashitaka ya jinai ya matumizi ya nguvu, kuhakikisha kwamba idadi kubwa ya raia iliyobaki haiuchukulii ujauzito kama kadi ya kumtoa mtu jela bure. ||| However, the message is for magistrates to follow the spirit of the law and grant this permission to those women not involved in violent crimes, to ensure that the rest of the civilian population doesn't see pregnancy as a get out of jail free card.
Katika visiwa vya Canary, kwa mujibu wa blogu ya Prisiones y penas, ambayo huandika kuhusu habari zinazohusu jela na magereza, wanawake wanaruhusiwa kuishi na watoto wao hadi umri wa miaka mitatu ndani ya selo zao, lakini wakiwa pamoja na wafungwa wenzao, kitu ambacho sio mazingira mazuri sana kwako. ||| In the Canary Islands, according to the Prisiones y Penas blog, which writes about the issues surrounding jails and prisons, women are allowed to keep their children of up to 3 years of age with them in their cells, but in the company of other inmates, which isn't the best environment.
Kwa hiyo, wanawake wajawazito au wanawake wenye watoto wenye umri wa chini ya miaka 3 huambiwa kuhusiana na kuingia kwenye magereza kuwa si vizuri kwa mtoto kukualia gerezani, na hupewa uchaguzi wa kumpeleka mtoto kwa wanafamilia wengine. ||| Thus, pregnant women or women with children under 3 are told upon entry to the prison that it isn't good for the child to grow up behind bars, and options are given for them to send the child off to family members.
Hali ni hii hii huko Peru na Urusi. ||| This is also the case in Peru and Russia.
Nchini Marekani, kuna magereza mawili tu yenye kuruhusu jambo hili, huko New York na Nebraska, kama ilivyoonyeshwa na mpiga picha maarufu Jane Evelyn Atwood kwenye insha ya picha zake tatu kwa ajili ya Shirika la kimataifa la Amnesty International, inayoitwa Too Much Time, ambapo alitembelea dazani nyingi za magereza kote duniani kurekodi na kuweka kumbukumbu za maisha ya wafungwa. ||| In the US, there are only two correctional facilities which allow for this, in New York and in Nebraska, as told by renowned photographer Jane Evelyn Atwood in her 3 part photo documentary for Amnesty International, called Too Much Time, where she visited dozens of prisons all over the world to record and document the lives of inmates.
Kwa nini mfumo wa magereza nchini Marekani hauruhusu, kwa ujumla, wanawake wenye watoto kubaki nao? ||| Why does the US correctional system not generally allow women with babies to keep them?
Atwood anaeleza kwamba kwa sababu ya mazingira ufungwa, hairuhusiwi. ||| Atwood explains that due to the hostage situation, it is not allowed.
Kwenye blogu ya Prison Photography wanaelezea madai haya: ||| In the Prison Photography Blog they address this claim:
Watoto hawahusishwi kwenye magereza yote isipokuwa mawili tu nchini Marekani. ||| Children are excluded from all but a couple of US prisons.
Tishio la usalama linatajwa kama sababu: mtoto ndani ya gereza ni dhaifu na atakuwa shabaha ya malengo maovu siku zote. ||| The security threat is cited as the reason: a child inside a prison is a constant vulnerable life and constant hostage target.
Madai yanaonekana kuwa hayana maana kwa kiasi fulani kwa unapofananisha na mifumo ya adhabu kwa nchi nyinginezo. ||| The claim seems a little bogus when penal systems of other countries are brought into consideration.
Insha ya Atwood kwenye wavuti ya Amnesty International inaonyesha mambo mawili, sehemu inayohusu taratibu za kujifungua huku umefungwa minyororo kama yalivyoelezwa kwenye Mtoto wa Vanessa na pia inaonyesha jambo jingine kuhusu mfumo wa magereza na umama, kwa kutumia picha za wanawake wakati mpigapicha akisoma insha kuhusu uzoefu wake wa kutembelea magereza huku akipiga picha. ||| The Atwood documentary in the Amnesty International site features both a section on the process of giving birth in shackles as told in Vanessa's Baby and another on prison systems and motherhood, with photographs of the women while the photographer reads an essay on her experiences visiting the prisons and taking the pictures.
Ujauzito kama zana ya mapatano? ||| Pregnancy as a bargaining tool?
Kwa nini haki za wanawake wajawazito gerezani zinatatanisha? ||| Why are rights for pregnant women in prison so controversial?

Katika Russia Today, idhaa ya matangazo ya Kirusi, mada hii inatajwa panapojadiliwa suala la watoto kuzaliwa na kulelewa katika mfumo wa magereza wa Kirusi: ||| In Russia Today, a Russian broadcasting channel, the subject is mentioned when discussing children born and raised in the Russian correctional system:
Wenye kutilia mashaka (suala hili) wanadhani akina mama wengine hupata ujauzito kwa makusudi ili tu kurahisisha maisha huko gerezani. ||| Skeptics think some mothers deliberately get pregnant simply to ease life in prison.
Ruhusa ya kwenda hospitali, halafu kuwa na ratiba iliyojaa muda mwingi na mwanao ñ ni afadhali kuliko kukaa kwenye seli ya magereza, wanadai. ||| Hospital leave, then lots of scheduled time with your child ñ it is all better than sitting in a stone cell, they claim.
Na kuna wanawake ambao wanaona kwamba kuwa na mimba ni njia pekee ya kukwepa hukumu, kama ilivyotokea mwezi Juni, pale mwanamama wa Kiingereza aliwekwa ndani na kuhukumiwa kifo huko Laos kwa sababu ya kusafirisha madawa ya kulevya akapata ujauzito gerezani na akanusurika kunyongwa, kwa sababu serikali ya Laos isingemnyonga mwanamama mjamzito. ||| And there are women for whom it seems that pregnancy is the only way to escape a sentence, as was the case back in June, when a British woman incarcerated and sentenced to death in Laos due to drug smuggling got pregnant in prison and escaped being executed, since the Laos government would not execute a pregnant woman.
Madai yaliyotolewa kwa mujibu wa jarida la Kiingereza la Daily Express, ni kwamba alipata ujauzito kwa kupandikiziwa mbegu za kiume ìili kupata hukumu nyepesi zaidiî ||| The claims made according to the Daily Express, a British newspaper, are that she got artificially inseminated ìto secure a more lenient termî.
Kwa maneno yao: Wanawake wanaeleza kuhusu watoto wao na maisha ya gerezani ||| In their words: Women tell of their children and prison life
Geraldin RodrÌguez, Mwajentina aliye kwenye jela za Ecuador kwa sababu ya biashara ya madawa ya kulevya anamueleza Marcos Brugiati, mwandishi mshiriki katika chapisho la mtandaoni linalohusiana na masuala ya sanaa liitwalo Plastica-Argentina, masimulizi kuhusu kuigiza na kufanya maonyesho ndani ya jela, kupata ujauzito gerezani na kumpata mwanae. ||| Geraldin RodrÌguez, an Argentinean spending time in an Ecuadorian jail due to drug trafficking tells Marcos Brugiati, a writer who contributes with the art related online publication Plastica-Argentina, the story about acting and performing in jail, getting pregnant in prison and having her child.
