Watu wengi miongoni mwa wale ambao wamekwishaona filamu hiyo ya Usov, kwa ufupi, walishtushwa mno na yale waliyoona. ||| Many of those who have already watched Usov's documentary were shocked by what they saw, to say the least.
Levko wa blogu ya the English-language Foreign Notes aliandika yafuatayo katika makala aliyopita jina la, Gereza la Lukyaniv lililogeuka kuwa tundu la jehanamuù: ||| Levko of the English-language Foreign Notes blog wrote this in a post entitled, The hell-hole that is Lukyaniv prisonù:
Mwandishi shupavu wa habari za uchunguzi wa kutoka TVi Konstyantyn Usov hivi karibuni alifaulu kuingiza kwa siri simu kadhaa za mkononi kwenye gereza linalosifika kwa ukatili la Lukyaniv, ambapo kuna kitengo cha uchunguzi maalumu, mahali ambapo alitiwa kizuizini, na ambapo bado anaendelea kushikiliwa. ||| The brave investigative journalist Konstyantyn Usov from TVi recently managed to smuggle several mobile phones into the notorious Lukyaniv investigative isolation unit where was detained, and where is still being held.
Katika filamu yake ya televisheni inayoweza kusababisha jinamizi inaweza kupatikana hapa. ||| His nightmarish television documentary can be seen here.
Hali katika baadhi ya vyumba vya gereza hilo ni mbaya mno za kutisha tafadhali usiitazame muda mfupi kabla ya kwenda kulala ||| The conditions in some of the cells are unimaginably bad diabolical don't watch it before going to bed 
Kumbuka, mahabusu wanaoonyeshwa bado hawajahukumiwa huenda wengi wao hawana hatia ingawa hata hivyo wamekuwa kizuizini kwa miaka mingi. ||| Remember, the inmates shown have not been tried or sentenced many may be innocent but may nevertheless be detained there for years.
Ni vigumu kuamini kwamba binadamu wanaweza kutendewa vibaya kiasi hicho tena katika taasisi ya serikali katika mji mkuu wa nchi ya kidemokrasi barani Ulaya katika karne ya 21 ni jambo linalotia kinyaa na aibu kubwa. ||| It is difficult to accept that human beings can be so maltreated in a state institution in the capital city of a European democracy in the 21st century utterly and absolutely shameful.
Gereza la Lukyanivska lilipata kufahamika kwa macho ya kimataifa mwaka jana, pale Waziri Mkuu wa zamani, Yulia Tymoshenko alipowekwa kizuizini katika gereza hilo na hasa wakati wa kesi yake. ||| Lukyanivska prison gained some international exposure last year, when ex-Prime Minister Yulia Tymoshenko was placed there during her trial.
Miriam Elder wa gazeti la The Guardian alizungumzia kuhusu taasisi hiyo ya mahabusu mnamo tarehe 16 Oktoba, 2011: ||| The Guardian's Miriam Elder described the detention facility on October 16, 2011:
Tymoshenko bado yupo katika gereza la Lukyanivska, ambalo linatumika zaidi kama kituo cha mahabusu wanaosubiri kesi zao. ||| Tymoshenko remains inside Lukyanivska, which functions mainly as a pre-trial detention centre.
Waziri Mkuu huyu wa zamani amewekwa kwenye chumba chenye ukubwa wa mita zipatazo 15 pamoja na wanawake wengine wawili, wote wakisubiri kesi za uhujumu uchumi. ||| She shares a 15 square meter space with two other women, both awaiting charges on economic crimes.
Kuna dirisha dogo ambalo limewekewa safu tatu za nondo. ||| There is a small window, covered with three sets of bars.
Hakuna maji ya moto na kuta nene za karne ya 19 zinafanya hali ndani ya gereza hili iwe ya baridi na yenye unyevunyevu. ||| There is no hot water and the thick walls of the 19th-century prison keep its interior cold and damp.
Tymoshenko anatumia muda wake wa siku kujisomea. ||| Tymoshenko spends her days reading.
Mwezi Desemba 2011, picha ya video iliyopigwa kwa siri na kuvujishwa ilimwonyesha Tymoshenko akiwa katika kitengo cha matibabu cha gereza la Lukyanivska. Video hiyo ilirushwa hewani kupitia televisheni na vilevile mitandao ya kiraia ya huko Ukraine. ||| In December 2011, a leaked video showing Tymoshenko at the medical wing of Lukyanivska prison was aired on TV and shared on social networks in Ukraine.
kwa upande wake Reuters ilitoa habari mnamo tarehe 15 Desemba: ||| Reuters reported on December 15:
Picha hiyo ya video ilikuwa moja kati ya mbili zilizorushwa hewani na televisheni ili kuonyesha kwamba Tymoshenko alikuwa akitendewa vema na kuwa aliishi maisha mazuri sawa na kwenye hoteli za kifahari. ||| The video clip was one of two aired on TV with the apparent aim of showing Tymoshenko was being well treated and living in conditions akin to those of a good hotel.
Katika picha hiyo, askari magereza wanaonekana wakishughulika kumsaidia mpiga picha za video kufanya kazi hiyo, kiasi hata cha kumusaidia kufunika tundu la ufunguo katika mlango wa kuingilia eneo hilo. ||| In the video, prison guards are actively helping the cameraman to shoot the film, even holding back a keyhole cover into the room for him.
Tyomoshenko mwenye umri wa miaka 51, alikuwa amefunikwa na mashuka, na alionyesha wazi kuwa hakufurahishwa na kitendo cha kuchukuliwa kwa filamu ile, ingawa maneno yake hayakuweza kusikika. ||| The 51-year-old Tymoshenko, who was mostly covered by bed-clothes, was clearly unhappy at being filmed, though her words were not audible.
Katika sehemu moja ya picha hiyo ya video, ambayo ilionyesha chumba kilicho na samani za maana ikiwa ni pamoja na jokofu, Tymoshenko anaweza kusikika akisema: Nilikuwa nimewekwa mahali penye hali mbaya sana, sitaki mwonyeshe picha hizi zinazodanganya kuhusu hali halisi sasa. ||| In another part of the footage, which showed a well-furnished room with a refrigerator, Tymoshenko can be heard saying: I was being kept before in unacceptable conditions and I don't want you to show this false picture now.ù 
Lakini katika filamu yake, Kostiantyn Usov, anaonyesha hali halisi ilivyo katika gereza la Lukyanivska, kama mahali ambapo maelfu ya raia wa Ukraine ambao hawana fursa ya kuonekana kwenye vyombo vya habari vya nyumbani na hata vile vya kimataifa, wanavyopitisha miaka katika mazingira ya mlundikano, na hali zisizo za kibinadamu wakati wanaposubiri hukumu zao. ||| In his documentary, Kostiantyn Usov shows the Lukyanivska prison the way it really is, as a place where thousands of Ukrainians with no access to domestic or international media spend years living in overcrowded, subhuman conditions as they await their verdicts.
Yeye aliandika akisema pale alipozungumzia utengenezaji wa filamu hiyo katika blogu yake Ukrainska Pravda: ||| He wrote this about the making of the film on his blog at Ukrainska Pravda:
Mahali ambapo watu wanahifadhiwa kama wanyama. ||| A place where people are kept as animals.
Gereza la Lukyanivska ni taasisi ya kuweka watu kizuizini. ||| Lukyanivska prison is a facility of preliminary detention.
Kuwekwa katika vyumba vyake visivyo na mwanga wala si adhabu, bali ni hatua ya kutoa kinga tu. ||| To be staying in its dark cells isn't a punishment, but a preventive measure.
Ndiyo kusema, yeyote anayeshukiwa kwa lolote anaweza kutupwa ndani yake, na katika Ukraine ya sasa, haina maana kwamba mtu huyo lazima awe mhalifu wa kweli. ||| That is, any suspect can be locked up here, and in contemporary Ukraine it absolutely does not mean that one has to be a real criminal.
Gereza la Lukyanivska linashika nafasi ya kwanza katika ripoti za ukatili, unyama, hali mbaya kwa maisha ya binadamu na vifo visivyo na maelezo katika vyumba vya gereza hilo, na hapa ndipo ambao utawala wa Rais Victor Yanukovych umekuwa ukiwaweka maadui wake na ndiyo sababu tulilifanya jambo la kuwaonyesha watu hali halisi ya Lukyanivka, kuwa lengo letu. ||| Lukyanivska prison occupies the first place in the number of reports of cruelty, torture, inhuman living conditions and mysterious deaths in prison cells, and this is where the regime of President Victor Yanukovych has been placing its enemies and this is why we have made it our goal to find a way to show people the real Lukyanivka.
Kuonyesha hali halisi, na si yale ambayo wao wanataka kutuonyesha tena kupitia vyombo vya habari wanavyovichagua wenyewe. ||| The real one, and not what they show to the select media.
Tuliunda mtandao wa wapelelezi wetu ndani ya gereza, ili kuhakikisha tuna watu wetu kwenye kila jengo, katika kila ghorofa kwenye mahabusu ya SIZO katika muda mfupi. ||| We created our own network of agents inside the prison, in order to have our own people in every building, on every floor of the SIZO in a minimal period of time.
Kutoka uraiani, tulipenyeza simu zenye uwezo wa kuchukua picha za video ili ziwafikie wapelelezi wetu, na mahabusu hao walitupatia vidokezo (kwa njia ya video) vya maisha yao, na polepole, kila video ikiwa na urefu wa sekunde 10 hadi 15, kwa kipindi cha miezi sita. ||| From the free outside, we smuggled mobile phones equipped with video cameras to each of our agents, and the inmates were sending us glimpses into their lives, little by little, 10 to 15 seconds at a time, for six months.
Usov amekuwa akipokea picha hizo alizotengenezea filamu iliyo kwenye blogu yake Ukrainska Pravda, na vilevile katika Facebook, Twita, YouTube na penginepo. ||| Usov has been receiving feedback on his film on his Ukrainska Pravda blog, as well as on Facebook, Twitter, YouTube and elsewhere.
Watu wengi wanamsifu Usov kwa ujasiri wake. ||| Many people praise Usov for his courage.
Ninaweza tu kufikiri kazi kubwa ambayo Usov na timu yake kutengeneza filamu hii walifanya, kazi yake hii haitapita bure, yeye ni mtu jasiri, walau tu tungekuwa na watu wengi zaidi kama yeye. ||| I can imagine what it took Usov and his team to make this film, his work will never be in vain, he is a brave person, if only there were more people like him.
Watu wengi wana wasiwasi juu ya usalama wa mwandishi huyu wa habari. ||| Many are concerned for the journalist's safety.
Kwenye Facebook, Roman Plechun aliandika: ||| On Facebook, Roman Plechun wrote:
Kostiantyn, je, huogopi kwamba utawalaù utaanza kukufuatilia? ||| Kostiantyn, aren't you afraid that the regimeù will come after you?
Ningependa tu kufahamu ulipata wapi ujasiri ili kufanya kazi hiyo! ||| I'd just like to understand how you found courage for this!
Mtumiaji wa YouTube anayejiita BenderZT aliandika hivi kuhusu yale yatakayotokana na filamu hiyo: ||| YouTube user BenderZT wrote this about the main implication of the film:
Kuna msemo mzuri katika hitimisho la filamu yenyewe, kwamba Gereza la Lukyanivska ni picha ndogo tu inayoonyesha hali halisi ilivyo katika nchi nzima. ||| A good phrase as the film's conclusion, that Lukyanivska prison is a micro-model of the country.
Ni jambo la kuhuzunisha kutokana na ukweli huu ||| Very sad to realize this 
Ni filamu inayotia huzuni sana kuitazama na kuona maovu na kupoteza maana kwa mfumo ambao haujali hata kidogo masuala ya utu. ||| Hard to watch it and see all the horror and meaninglessness of the system that is indifferent to the human being.
Na jambo la kutisha zaidi ni kwamba, mfumo huu umetengenezwa na kuendelezwa na binadamu wenywe. ||| And the most terrible thing is that this system has been created by human beings and is being maintained by human beings too.
Kuhusu blogu ya Usov Ukrainska Pravda, mtumiaji Facebook anayejiita Lyubomyr alijaribu kutoa ufafanuzi kuhusiana na ukatili unaoshtua wa maisha katika gereza la Lukyanivska kama yalivyoonyeshwa kwenye filamu: ||| On Usov's Ukrainska Pravda blog, Facebook user Lyubomyr offered this explanation for the shocking cruelty of life at Lukyanivska shown in the film:
Kusema ukweli, maslahi ya kifedha wanayopata askari magereza si sababu ya pekee kwa hali mbaya iliyo kwenye mahabusu ya SIZO. ||| Actually, financial gain of the prison staff isn't the only reason for such horrible conditions at the SIZO.
Sababu nyingine ya hali hiyo ya kutisha katika SIZO ni kutengeneza mazingira yasiyovumilika ili kwamba mtu anayewekwa humo pengine angebembeleza ili walau ahamishiwe kwenye magereza ya kweli, ambapo hali zina unafuu fulani. ||| The other goal of the SIZO is to create conditions so unbearable that a person would be basically begging to be transferred to the real prison, where the conditions are somewhat better after all.
Kwa mfano, kama kuna mtu mwenye kesi ambayo haina ushahidi wa maana ili kumpata na hatia, lakini wakati huo huo watawala wanataka kuona kwamba anakutwa na hatia kwa ajili ya maslahi yao, mathalani kujipatia sifa kwa kesi ambazo zimepatiwa ufumbuzi. ||| Say, there is someone whose case lacks any evidence needed to prove guilt, but the authorities need to convict this person for their own benefit, to improve the statistics of solved cases, for example.
Kwa hiyo, wanamsweka mtu katika mahabusu ya SIZO, na baada ya miezi michache ya kipindi cha mateso, mtu huyo anakuwa tayari hata kutoa maelezo ya kujikandamiza mwenyewe, anatoa kauli inayomtia mwenyewe hatiani, anakiri kutenda jambo asilolitenda ili tu apate fursa ya kuondoka kutoka kwenye mahabusu ya SIZO, hata kama ni kwenda kufungwa gerezani. ||| So they put this person into the SIZO, and after a few months of what in fact is torture, he or she is ready to testify against him/herself, submit a self-incriminating statement, admit guilt completely just to have a chance to get out of the SIZO, even if it means getting out to prison.
Katika maoni mengine kwenye blogu ya Usov, Ukrainska Pravda, mtumiaji skilachi aliandika kwamba: ||| In another comment on Usov's Ukrainska Pravda blog, user skilachi wrote this:
Karibu kila kitu kiko kama kilivyokuwa miaka nane iliyopita. ||| Almost everything is the way it was eight years ago.
Bado ninakumbuka kila moja ya siku 254 nilizowekwa mle. ||| I still remember each of the 254 days that I spent there.
Baada ya kuachiwa kwangu huru, nilitamani: kwamba kila mfanyakazi wa siku za usoni wa Wizara ya Mambo ya Ndani, ofisi ya mwendesha mashtaka, mahakama au taasisi yoyote inayohusina na kuweka watu rumande, basi waonjeù hata kwa miezi michache maisha ya kwenye taasisi hiyo kabla kuanza kazi kama walinzi wa sheria na mfumo wa mahakama. ||| Upon my release I wished for this: that every future employee of the Ministry of Internal Affairs, prosecutor's office, court or any other entity that locks people up, had an internshipù for at least a few months at this facility prior to assuming their positions in law enforcements and the judiciary.
Pengine wangejifunza kutumia njia mbadala ya kuchukua hatua za kinga dhidi ya watuhumiwa. ||| Maybe then they'd view the use of preventive measures towards suspects and the accused differently.
Lakini hii ni kama vile kuota ndoto za Alinacha. ||| But this is just wishful thinking.
Kwa wale ambao wamewahi kuonja jehanamu hii, nawatakia nyote afya njema. ||| To those who have been through this hell, my best wishes of health.
Kwa wale watakaoshindwa kuepa kuingia humo, kumbukeni kujitahidi kubaki mkiwa na utu wenu. ||| To those who fail to avoid this, remember to always remain human beings.
Yaelekea kuna mwitikio kutoka kwenye mamlaka kuhusiana na filamu ya Usov. ||| There seems to have been no reaction from the authorities to Usov's film yet.
Idara ya Magereza ya Ukraine, hata hivyo, ilitoa tamko kupitia taarifa kwa vyombo vya habari mnamo tarehe 2 Aprili, inayosomeka kama njia ya kupuuziaù ujumbe kama ule wa Usov: ||| The State Penitentiary Service of Ukraine, however, issued a statement through its press service on April 2, which reads like a preemptive strikeù type of message to journalists like Usov:
Kyiv SIZO taasisi yenye mvuto zaidi kwa vyombo vya habari ||| Kyiv SIZO the most interesting facility for the mass media
Katika siku za hivi karibuni, kumekuwa na taarifa, maoni na habari za hapa na pale zinazotolewa na vyombo vya habari kuhusiana na kazi za taasisi za Idara ya Magereza. ||| Recently, there have been more and more information, commentaries and random stories appearing in the mass media about the work of the Penitentiary Service facilities.
Nyingi ya hizi ni maoni kuhusu hali, ambazo kwamo, wale watu waliokamatwa na wale wengine waliotiwa hatiani wanamoishi, na pia kuhusu vitendo vya wafanyakazi wa taasisi hizo. ||| The majority of these stories comment on the conditions in which the arrested and convicted persons are being kept, as well as on the actions by the penitentiary facilities staff.
Uchambuzi wa machapisho hayo filamu unaonyesha kukosa ujuzi na kutotimiza sharti la kupata maoni ya upande wa pili, na mara nyingine kupuuzia kabisa kwa taaluma ya habari na waandishi. ||| The analysis of the publications and films shows lack of competence and objectivity, and sometimes outright unhidden bias of the journalists.
Kwa sababu hii, wawakilishi wa idara ya magereza wanakana taarifa zote zilizotangazwa au kutolewa kama maoni ya ziada zinazoihusu. ||| Due to this, penitentiary service representatives systematically refute the published information or provide additional commentary on it.
Kuhusu picha zilizotolewa hivi karibuni kuhusu gereza la Lukyanivska katika ngazi ya kimataifa, LEvko wa Foreign Notes anaunganisha na habari hii iliyokuwa kwenye gazeti la Kyiv Post kuhusu mkutano uliofanyika tarehe 3 Aprili kati ya wawakilishi wa Freedom House na mmoja wa mahabusu wenye hadhi ya juu zaidi aliye SIZO, waziri wa zamani wa mambo ya ndani, Yuri Lutsenko. ||| As for Lukyanivska prison's most recent international exposure, LEvko of Foreign Notes links to this Kyiv Post item on the April 3 meeting of Freedom House representatives with one of the SIZO's highest-ranking current inmates, ex-minister of internal affairs Yuri Lutsenko.
Watu kutoka Freedom House waliomtembelea Yuriy Lutsenko gerezani siku ya Jumanne hawana budi kutazama video ya Usov baada ya kutembelea gereza hilo: Idara ya Ukraine ya Magereza na Mahabusu ilisisitiza kwamba wageni hao walisema kwamba Ukraine ilichukua hatua kuhakikisha kwamba hali katika mahabusu na magereza na zahanati zinazoshughulikia mahabusu zilikuwa zikienda sambamba na viwango vya kimataifa.ù ||| The Freedom House guys who visited Yuriy Lutsenko at the prison on Tuesday should check out Usov's video. After their visit: The Ukrainian State Penitentiary Service stressed that the visitors noted that Ukraine took measures to bring conditions for detention and medical treatment for detainees in line with international standards.ù
Tazama Picha za Afghanistan Ambazo Huwa Huzioni ||| Sharing Photos of the Afghanistan You Never See
Miongo ya vita na ugaidi vimeiweka Afghanistan katika kundi la nchi hatari zaidi kuishi duniani. ||| The decades of war and terrorism have placed Afghanistan among the world's most dangerous countries.
Pamoja na hatua za mafanikio zilizofikiwa na nchi hiyo tangu kuondolewa kwa wa-Taliban mwaka 2001, vyombo vingi vya habari vinavyoandika habari za Afghanistan kwa ujeuri tu vimejikita katika masuala hasi kama vile milipuko ya mabomu, mashambulizi ya kujitoa muhanga na kujeruhiwa kwa watu. ||| Despite the progress made by the country since the ousting of the Taliban in 2001, most media writing about Afghanistan focus stubbornly on negative issues such as bomb blasts, suicide attacks, and casualties.
Ripoti katika vyombo hivyo zinaonyesha picha za kuogofya ambazo husababisha watu wengi kughairi kabisa mpango wa kuitembelea nchi hiyo iliyoathirika vibaya na mapigano lakini kwa asili ikiwa ni nchi nzuri sana. ||| Reports in such media feature terrifying pictures that lead most people to never want to visit the war-torn but very beautiful country.
Hii ndiyo sababu kazi ya Antony Loveless, mwanablogu Antony Loveless, mwandishi huru wa habari na mpiga picha wa Ki-Ingereza, inaleta tofauti kubwa. ||| This is why the work of Antony Loveless, a freelance British journalist and photographer, makes so much difference.
Tangu mwezi Machi 2012, Loveless amekuwa akiweka picha anazopiga katika safari zake nchini Afghanistan kupitia mtandao wa twita, kwa kutumia alama ishara aliyoitengeneza yeye. ||| Since March 2012, Loveless has been posting photos from his trips to Afghanistan on Twitter, using the hashtag he invented.
Akioongea na mwandishi wa Global Voices kuhusu alama ishara hiyo ya twita, Loveless alisema: ||| Speaking to Global Voices about the hashtag, Loveless said:
Nina jalada lenye picha zaidi ya 2,000 zilizopigwa katika safari zangu tatu nilizofanya nchini Afghaniistan katika miaka ya hivi karibuni na ili kuweka kumbukumbu hizo, niliamua kutengeneza alama ishara ya. ||| I have a portfolio of over 2,000 images shot on three trips to Afghanistan in recent years and to keep track of them, I conceived of the rather unwieldy hashtag.
Msichana katika Ziwa. ||| The Girl in the Lake.
Akiogelea kujipooza mwili baada ya jua kali la mchana. ||| Taking a dip to stay cool under the unforgiving midday sun.
Picha ya Antony Loveless, imetumiwa kwa ruhusa. ||| Image by Antony Loveless, used with permission.
eneo Kijani's 'nchini Afghastan', pana lenye rutuba, lililolimwa pembezoni mwa Bonde la Mto Helmand. ||| Afghanistan's 'green zone', a stretch of fertile, cultivated ground along the Helmand River Valley.
Uzuri usiomithilika wa Ziwa Kajaki kusini mwa Afghanistani, kama unavyoonekana ukiwa juu kwa ndege ya Royal Air Force Chinnok. ||| The stunning beauty of Kajaki Lake in southern Afghanistan, seen from a Royal Air Force Chinook.
Alama ishara hiyo ya Loveless ilitumiwa pia na Sajenti Alex Ford, wa Royal Air Force, aliishi kwenye jimbo la Hilmand nchini Afghanistan kwa muda wa miezi sita mwaka 2011. ||| Loveless hashtag was picked up by the Royal Air Force Sergeant Alex Ford, who spent six months in 2011 in Afghanistan's Hilmand Province.
Akielezea maoni yake kuhusu alama ishara hiyo ya twita, Ford anaandikakwenye Jarida la Warfare: ||| Sharing his views about the hashtag, Ford writes in Warfare Magazine:
Tumekuwa tukijihusisha na masuala ya Afghanistan kwa takribani miaka 11 sasa, na imekuwa kawaida kuona picha za vita kutoka hapa. ||| We have been involved in Afghanistan for almost 11 years now, and it has become commonplace to see images of the war back here.
Lakini picha hizo kwa ujumla huwa zinaonyesha upande hasi wa mgogoro nchini humo. ||| But generally those images tend to be more about the negative side of the conflict there.
Picha za majeneza yaliyofunikwa bendera yakiingizwa Wootton Bassett au kutoka brize Norton picha za mwanajeshi anayetabasamu, lakini maelezo chini yake yakitoa tarehe alipofariki dunia. ||| Pictures of flag-draped coffins driving through Wootton Bassett or out of Brize Norton a picture of a soldier smiling, but the caption underneath giving the date he died.
Inasikitisha sana, wengi wa wa-Ingereza wanaounga mkono wanawake na akina dada walio kwenye eneo la tukio hawana taarifa halisi za habari za vita inayoendelea kule; habari ambayo inatokana na Afghanistan yenyewe. ||| Sadly, the majority of the British population that supports the lads and lasses on the ground have no real insight into the story of the war out there; the story that is Afghanistan.
Watoto wa nchi hiyo wakiwa tayari kuzungumza na Paras anayeondoka eneo hilo la kutua kwa Helkopta. ||| Local children ready to chat to Paras leaving the Helicopter Landing Site.
Watoto wa ki-Afghanistan wakionyesha vitabu na kalamu walizopewa na UNICEF darasani kwake. ||| Afghan kids with UNICEF-donated books and pens in a classroom.
Alama ishara hiyo imekuwa maarufu kwa wale wanaosafiri kwenda Afghanistan kubadilishana picha ambazo watu nje ya nchi hiyo huziona mara chache katika vyombo vya habari. ||| The hashtag has become a popular photo tag for those who travel to Afghanistan to share the images that people outside of the country rarely see in conventional media.
Mtoto wa ki-Afghan akionekana tayari kutumia kamera. ||| An Afghan child seems ready to be on camera.
Hivi karibuni,Iqbal Ahmad Oruzgani, mpiga picha kutoka Afghanistan ameanza pia kuweka picha kwenye alama ishara hiyo hiyo ya mtandao wa twita kwa mtazamo tofauti. ||| Lately, Iqbal Ahmad Oruzgani, a photographer from Afghanistan has also begun posting photos under the hashtag to show Afghanistan from a different perspective.
Harusi za pamoja zilizoandaliwa kwa ajili ya kufungisha ndoa za makumi ya maarusi huko Daikundi, katikati ya Afghanistan. ||| Collective wedding organized for tens of couples in Daikundi, central Afghanistan.
Harusi za pamoja zimekuwa maarufu nchini humo kwa sababu hupunguza gharama za harusi kwa kila familia ya maarusi. ||| Collective weddings have becoming very popular in the country because they help lessen the cost of wedding for each individual family.
Wasichana wa ki-Afghan wakisoma kitabu cha shule mbele ya duka lililofungwa. ||| Young Afghan girls reading a school book in front of a closed shop.
Kipindi cha baridi katika wilaya ya Behsud iliyopo katika Jimbo la Maidan Waedak. ||| Winter in Behsud District of Maidan Wardak Province.
Kila picha iliyowekwa katika alama ishara hiyo ya twita hutwitiwa tena (retweeted) na mamia ya watumiaji wa twita, kuwawezesha wapiga picha hao kupata hadhira kubwa zaidi. ||| Every photo shared under this hashtag is retweeted by hundreds of Twitter users, giving the photographers a very wide audience.
Akizungumza na Global Voices, Antony Loveless anasema: ||| Speaking to Global Voices, Antony Loveless says:
Watumiaji wasiohesabika wa twita wanasema hayo ni matumizi mazuri zaidi ya alama ishara za twita, kuliko ilivyopata kutokea, na hivi sasa niko kwenye mazungumzo kuchapisha kitabu kinachotokea na alama habari ya twita baada ya watu wengi mno kuonyesha nia ya kukinunua ikiwa kitachapishwa. ||| Countless tweeters have said its the best use of a hashtag on twitter, ever, and I am currently in talks to produce a book based on the hashtag after countless people expressed an interest in buying one.
Sri Lanka: Kulipia Vyombo Vya Kimataifa Vya Habari kwa Ajili ya Uchaguzi wa Ndani ||| Sri Lanka: Paying Global Media For Local Elections
Kampeni kabambe ya Rais wa Sri Lanka aliye madarakani, Mahinda Rajapakshe inajumuisha manunuzi ya nafasi za matangazo katika tovuti mashuhuri za vyombo vya habari duniani. ||| Sri Lanka's incumbent president Mahinda Rajapakshe's aggressive re-election campaign includes purchasing banner ads on leading global media sites.
Groundviews anahoji sababu ya kuvilipa vyombo vya habari vya kimataifa kwa ajili ya uchaguzi wa ndani ya nchi. ||| Groundviews questions what is the point of paying global media for local elections.
Gumzo la moja kwa moja kuhusu Virusi vya ukimwi na Ukimwi mtandaoni Tarehe 6 machi ||| Blogging Positively: Live Chat about HIV/AIDS on March 6
Mradi wa Rising Voices na Global Voices wanaandaa gumzo la moja kwa moja mtandaoni kwa wanablogu na wanaharakati siku ya Ijumaa mwezi wa tatu mwaka huu (saa 11 jioni kwa saa za Nairobi) mada kuu ikiwa jinsi ya kublogu na kuongeza uelewa na habari kuhusu virusi vya ukimwi na Ukimwi. ||| Rising Voices and Global Voices are holding a live online chat for bloggers and activists on Friday March 6, 2009 (5 pm Nairobi time) on how to use blogging to improve awareness and information about HIV/AIDS.
Kila mmoja anakaribishwa ||| Everyone is welcome.
Jinsi ya kujiunga:Bonyeza kingo hapo juu tumia jina lako.Kisha chagua chumba utakacho kujiunga kwa kubonyeza ingia.Baada ya kuingia chagua ukubwa wa maandishi upande wa kushoto wa kiwambo cha tarakishi yako, jiunge katika gumzo ||| Then select the room you want to join by clicking enter. Once in the room, select a font color on the left side of the screen, and join the chat.
Gumzo la tarehe 6 mwezi wa 3 litajenga mada iliyoletwa katika majadiliano yaliofanikiwa wiki iliyopita. ||| The March 6th chat will build on topics brought up in last week's successful online discussion.
Gumzo la tarehe 27 mwezi wa pili lilitoa tamko kama vile umuhimu wa kublogu kwa watu walioathirika na virusi vya ukimwi na jukumu katika upelekaji na ushawishi wa maarifa,lakini kikubwa lililenga kwenye muongozo wa kublogu vyema ,muongozo ulitengenezwa na Global Voices kutoa ushauri tunu jinsi ya kublogu kuhusu masuala ya Virusi vya Ukimwi na Ukimwi. ||| The February 27th chat addressed issues such as why blogging can be important for people affected by HIV/AIDS and the vital roles of mentoring and advocacy, but it mainly focused on the Blogging Positively Guide, a guide being created by Global Voices to provide valuable advice on how to blog about HIV/AIDS issues.
Muongozo huo bado ni kazi inayooendelea, kwa hiyo tunatafuta msaada kutengeneza na kutoa matokeo. ||| The Guide is a work-in-progress, so we are looking for help to create it and/or to give feedback.
Kwa wale waliokuwa na nia au waliokwisha blogu kuhusu maafa wanahimizwa kushiriki katika gumzo wiki hii, hasa wale wanaoishi au walioathirika na virusi vya ukimwi. ||| Those interested in or already blogging about the pandemic are encouraged to participate in this week's chat, particularly those living with and/or affected by HIV/AIDS.

Pia kuna mada nyingine ambazo utataka kujadili wakati wa gumzo,tafadhali weka maoni chini.Natumaini mtashirikiana nasi tarehe 6 mwezi wa tatu ||| If there are other topics that you would like to discuss during the chat, please add comments below. Hope you can join us on March 6!
Saudi Arabia: Kina Mama Huru ||| Saudi Arabia: Independent women
WAKATI kukiwa hakuna shaka kwamba kuna vizuizi kwa wanawake waishio Saudi Arabia, havifanani na taswira iliyojengwa na wageni dhidi ya taifa hilo. ||| While there are no doubt restrictions for women living in Saudi Arabia, they do not necessarily match the oppressive image that many foreigners have of the country.
Katika makala hii tunao ushauri kwa wakina mama wanaotaka kutembelea jiji la Jeddah wakiwa peke yao, kuna muhtasari wa hoteli za kina mama pekee jijini Riyadh, na wito kwa wageni wote wanajihisi kuzungumza kwa niana ya kina mama wanaokandamizwa wa Saudia. ||| In this post we have advice for women wanting to visit Jeddah alone, a review of a women-only hotel in Riyadh, and a plea to those foreigners who feel they want to speak on behalf of oppressed Saudi women.
Tunaanza na Hala, ambaye anaishi Marekani hivi sasa, anayetoa ushauri kwa marafiki zake akinamama wasio na waume watakaotaka kutembelea jiji la Jeddah kwa mara yao ya kwanza: ||| We start with Hala, currently living in the US, who is giving advice to a single female friend visiting Jeddah for the first time:
Wanawake katika jiji la Jeddah huvaa gauni lijulikanalo kama Abaya, gauni hili hupaswa kuvaliwa juu ya mavazi mengine hivyo vaa nguo nyepesi za ndani haswa wakati wa majira ya kiangazi. ||| Women in Jeddah are dressed in an outside gown called Abayaù, it supposed to be worn over clothes so dress lightly beneath it especially in the summer.
Ushungi si lazima kwa akina mama wageni lakini ni vazi linalopendekezwa kuvaliwa (kwa ajili ya usalama na kuepuka usumbufu usiokuwa wa lazima) katika maeneo ya kiutamaduni. ||| The scarf however, is not a must for a female visitor in Jeddah but a preferred thing to wear (for safety and convenience) in traditional places.
Kuna maeneo mbalimbali ya kuyaona jijini Jeddah, ninapendekeza Balad, jiji la kale la Jeddah, likiwa na majengo yaliyosanifiwa kizamani, Jengo la Naseef ni mfano mmojawapo wa majengo ya kale. ||| There are a variety of places to see in Jeddah, I would suggest the Balad, the old city of Jeddah, with its historical architecture and old houses, Naseef house is a good example of one.
Unaweza kununua bidhaa za kitamaduni za kale kutoka katika maduka ya kizamani na ukafurahia marashi ya Kiarabu kama vile Udi Bukhour, vilevile kuna bidhaa za kazi za mikono za kitamaduni kama balbu, fanusi, tende, pipi na vitambaa vya rangi mbalimbali. ||| You can purchase traditional goodies from the old shops and enjoy the aroma of Arabic perfumes like Oud and Bukhour, theres also the traditional handcrafts like the light bulbs or fanoos lantern, the dates, the sweets and the textiles with various colors.
Pia kuna barabara maarufu jijini Jeddah iliyokatiza ufukweni mwa bahari. ||| Then, theres the famous Jeddah Corniche.
Napendekeza upite katika barabara hiyo mapema alfajiri au jioni saa 12 ili uweze kujionea maumbile ya kupendeza baharini, pia kuna chemchem ya baharini, moja ya chemchem zilizoko juu zaidi kuliko nyingine yoyote duniani. ||| I suggest visiting it early in the morning or at 6pm to see the open air sculptures along the sea side, theres also Jeddah sea-fountain, one of the highest fountains in the world.
Kuna machaguo mbalimbali ya vyakula katika barabara ya kupendeza ufukweni mwa bahari, kuanzia migahawa ya ya anasa mpaka maduka ya vyakula vya haraka au hata vijiduka vidogo vya biskuti na chipsi. ||| There is a variety of food choices along the corniche from fancy eating in restaurants to fast food or even small booths for biscuits and chips.
Wenyeji hukuketi katika ufukweni kwa masaa na watoto wao wakicheza karibu yao huku wakiwaangalia wapita njia. ||| The local people would sit for hours by the sea side with their children playing around and watching the passersby.
Kwa ushauri zaidi wa Hala kuhusiana na unachotaka kukiona jijini Jeddah, angalia hapa. ||| For more of Halas advice of what to see in Jeddah, see here.
Wakati huo huo bloga American Bedu, ambaye ni Mmarekani anayeishi Saudi Arabia, anatueleza kile anachokifikiri kuhusiana na hoteli za kina mama pekee jijini Riyadh. ||| Meanwhile American Bedu, an American living in Saudi Arabia, tells us what she thinks of a women-only hotel in Riyadh:
Hoteli ya Al Luthan na bafu lake ni hoteli ya kwanza kabisa ya wanawake pekee ya aina yake jijini Riyadh. ||| The Al Luthan hotel and spa is the first women only facility of its kind in Riyadh.
Ni hoteli ya kifahari na ina bafu la chemchem maalumu kwa wanawake pekee. ||| It is a luxurious hotel and spa for women only.
Ni hoteli ya huduma zote yenye kutoa huduma za uhakika na yenye kutoa malazi salama. ||| It is a full service hotel and spa offering deluxe, comfortable and safe accommodations.
Al Luthan inapokea wageni wa kike kutoka Saudia na wasio Wasudia. ||| Al Luthan welcomes both Saudi and non-Saudi females.
Hivi sasa baadhi ya wanawake wamezungumza na vyombo vya abari wakisema kuwa kuzinduliwa Al Luthan ni mojawapo ya upigani hatua nyuma. ||| Now some women have spoken out to the media that the opening of Al Luthan is a step backwards.
Kwa mujibu wa wanawake hawa, wanaona kama ni kupiga hatua kuelekea nyuma kwa ufalme wa taifa hilo kutokana na ukweli kwamba tayari kuna ubaguzi na siyo tu kwamba wanawake wana haki kidogo lakini kwa kushabikia na kuafiki uanzishwaji wa hoteli ya wanawake peke yao yenye eneo la kuogea inarudisha nyuma harakati za kina mama kudai haki. ||| According to these women, they see it as a backwards movement for the Kingdom due to the fact that there is already so much enforced segregation and women not only have few rights but promoting and endorsing a womens only hotel and spa further diminishes women from receiving rights.
Pengine nimo kwenye kundi dogo katika jamii, lakini nachukua mtazamo mbadala. ||| Maybe I am in the minority but I take the opposite view.
Al Luthan siyo hoteli ya kipekee ikilinganishwa na hoteli nyingine duniani. ||| Al Luthan is not unique when compared to the rest of the world.
Hoteli za wanawake au hoteli zinazotenga safu nzima ya ghorofa kwaa jili ya wanawake zipo karibu katika kila jiji kubwa (na hata kwenye miji isiyo mikubwa) duniani. ||| Women hotels or women-only floors are actually common in most major cities (and some not so major) all over the world.
Siku za nyuma wakati nilipokuwa nikisafiri safari nyingi za kimataifa, nilikuwa nikifurahia kupanga katika hoteli zenye safu maalumu kwa ajili ya wanawake pekee. Haswa katika majiji ya kigeni ambayo hayakuzoea kuwa na wafanyabiashara wanawake wanaosafiri peke yao. ||| Back in earlier times when I was doing a lot of international travel, I enjoyed staying on a women-only floor, especially when in foreign cities which were not as accustomed to business women traveling alone.
Kwa hiyo mimi sioni kama kuanzishwa kwa hoteli hii maalumu kwa wanawake kuwa ni hatua ya kurudi nyuma asilani bali chaguo jema kwa wanawake kuwa nalo ndani ya falme. ||| So to me, I do not see a womens only hotel as a step backward at all but another nice option to have for women in the Kingdom.
Bloga kutoka Riyadh, SweetAnger amechoshwa na wageni wanaodhani kuwa wanawake wa Kisaudia wanakandamizwa, wakati hawajui lolote kuhusu maisha yao au jamii: ||| Riyadh blogger SweetAnger is fed up of foreigners assuming that Saudi women are oppressed, while knowing nothing about their lives or society:
Basi, nilikuwa nikitafiti mtandaoni kitu kimoja au kingine nikakutana na ujumbe kuhusu ripota aliyekuwa Saudia ambaye ni mwanamke na hivyo hakuruhusiwa kukaa kwenye sehemu ya wanaume ndani ya mgahawa wa Starbucks. ||| So I was googling one thing or another when I found a post about the abject horror of a reporter in Saudi who was female and was therefore not permitted to stay in the men's section of Starbucks.
Kitu kilichonishika zaidi siyo ile makala yenyewe, lakini maoni. ||| Now what grabbed my attention wasn't the article itself, but the comments.
 Nataka ieleweke kwamba Saudi siyo mahema machache yanayounganishwa na ngamia wanaorandaranda, na wanaume wenye vilemba waimbao Allah o akbarù huku wakiwabaka wanawake kwa sababu ni haki yao na wanamiliki nyumba ya harimu yenye vigoli si chini ya 20. ||| Just so we're clear, Saudi is not a bunch of tents stuck together with roaming camels, men in turbans singing Allah o akbarù raping women cause its their right and having a harem of no less then 20.
Oh, na pia hatutahiri wanawake wetu, hilo ni jambo la hovyo na ni kosa katika ngazi nyingi. ||| Oh and we don't circumcise our women, man thats just nasty and wrong on too many levels.
Wanawake hawafungiwi nyumbani na yeyote yule ambaye kwamba hilo ni jambo la utamaduni wa familia na siyo nchi, upo? ||| Women are not locked up at home and any who are is a matter of the family culture not the country, still with me?
Hatuko nyuma nyie mafidhuli, sisi ni wahafidhina, yaani, kama unapotaka kwenda kujichanganya na mtu wa jinsia tofauti kuna maeneo maalumu. ||| We're not backwards you morons, we're conservative, i.e. if you want to go and mingle with the opposite sex you go to a specific place.
Sasa hoja yangu ya msingi hapa ni kwamba hivi tangu lini mmeanza kuhukumu watu: Fungeni Starbucks!! ||| Now my more important point is, since when do you get off judging people: Close Starbucks!!
Zisiwe na sehemu zinazokaribisha familiaù, hapana samahani? ||| They shouldn't support them by opening families sectionsù, excuse me?
Silalamiki na ninahitaji kahawa yangu, tuache utani, POTEENI MBALI, sikukodi mtu yeyote awe msemaji wangu. ||| I'm not complaining, and I need my coffee, so seriously man, GET LOST, I didnt hire anyone to be my speaker.
Kwa wale ambao bado mnashawishika kwamba sisi ni taifa kandamizi na kwamba sisi wanawake masikini tunahitaji kufunzwa namna ya kupambana na kama sivyo vyema vyema endeleeni kutupigania, ngojeni niwape maelezo mafupi namna siku ya kawaida inavyokuwa jijini Riyadh. ||| For those of you who are still convinced we are an oppressed nation and us poor poor women need to be taught how to fight back and if not well go ahead and fight for us, let me give you a little review of what a regular day in Riyadh is like.
Jana niliamka nikatengeneza kahawa yangu nikatinga vazi langu la abaya (kama unaona hili linatisha kufikirika, lifikirie kama jaketi), nikamchukua malaika wangu mdogo, nikaingia ndani ya gari yangu iendeshwayo na dereva ndani yake, nikamshusha binti yangu, halafu nikaenda kazini. ||| Now yesterday I wake up, make my coffee get dressed put my abaya on (if its too horrific to think about this, think of it as a jacket), pick up my little angel, get in my chauffeured car a.k.a. driver included, drop my girl off, and go to work.
Mida ya saa 7:30 napata chakula cha mchana na marafiki zangu wa kike kutoka mgahawa wa Subway, halafu nikarejea kazini na kutoka saa 10:30 jioni, narejea nyumbani, napumzika, naoga natinga mavazi yangu, namsubiri dereva anipeleke mgahawa wa Wachina kwani nilikuwa nimewakaribisha marafiki zangu wa kike. ||| By 1:30 I'm having lunch from Subway with the girls, then go back to work and leave at 4:30, go home, relax, take a shower, get dressed, wait for the driver to take me to the Chinese place since I invited the girls out.
Nafika pale mida ya saa 3:45 hivi halafu naondoka kama saa 6, nafika nyumbani, naingia mtandaoni, naangalia facebook na hotmail, halafu naingia kitandani saa 8. ||| Get there around 9:45 and leave around 12, get home, get online, check my facebook and hotmail, then hit the sack by 2am.
MUNGU WANGU, JINAMIZI GANI HILI, NINAWEZAJE KUISHI MAISHA YA KIKANDAMIZWA NAMNA HII! ||| OH MY GOD, WHAT HORROR, HOW CAN I LIVE A LIFE SO OPPRESSED!
Hoja yangu ni kwamba baadhi ya watu hawana welewa kuhusu nini kinaendelea ndani ya maisha yetu na bado wanafikiri wana haki ya kuamua na kuwa wakuu. ||| My point is, some people have no knowledge about what goes on in our life yet they deem it their right to judge and be almighty.
Tuko tofauti, naam, na kwa kuwa tuko tofauti na vile ambavyo unafikiri ni sawa haitufanyi sisi kuwa wabaya au wenye makosa inatufanya sisi kuwa sisi. ||| We're different, hell yeah, being different from what you think is right doesn't make us bad or wrong it makes us us.
Kabiliana na ukweli huo au jitoe. ||| Deal with it and butt out.
Afrika ya Kusini: Matumizi ya Simu za Viganjani Kupambana na UKIMWI ||| South Africa: Using Cell Phones To Combat AIDS
Afrika ya Kusini imegundua silaha mpya katika vita dhidi ya VVU/UKIMWI simu za viganjani. ||| South Africa has found a new weapon in its fight against HIV/AIDS cell phones.
Kwenye mchakato mpya, jumbe za maandishi zitakuwa zikitumwa kila siku kuwahamasisha Wa-Afrika ya Kusini kwenda kupimwa na kutibiwa ugonjwa huo. ||| A new initiative will be sending free text messages daily to encourage South Africans to get tested and treated for the disease.
Mradi huo, unaoitwa Mradi wa Masiluleke, ulitangazwa rasmi wiki iliyopita wakati wa kongamano la Pop!Tech 2008 huko Maine, Marekani. ||| The project, called Project Masiluleke, was announced last week at the Pop!Tech 2008 conference in Maine, U.S.A.
Mradi huo umerahisishwa na mteremko unaotokana na umaarufu wa simu za viganjani nchini Afrika ya Kusini, na unatumia simu hizo za viganjani kupambana na idadi kubwa ya VVU na kifua kikuu. ||| It takes advantage of the popularity of cell phones in South Africa, using them to fight the country's high rates of HIV and tuberculosis.
Sehemu ya kwanza ya mradi huo itatuma takriban jumbe za bure zipatazo milioni moja kwa umma wa kawaida kila siku kwa mwaka mmoja, wakiuasa umma kwenda kwenye vituo vya VVU na kifua kikuu. ||| The first part of the project will send the general public approximately one million free text messages daily for a year, urging them to call HIV and TB call centers.
Jumbe hizo zitatumwa kama sehemu ya jumbe zinazoitwa Tafadhali Nipigie Simuù, ambayo ni aina ya ujumbe unaotumiwa sana katika Afrika. ||| These messages will be sent as part of Please Call Meù messages, a type of text messaging widely used across Africa.
White African anafafanua mradi huo pamoja na teknolojia yake: ||| White African elaborates on the project and this technology:
Gustav Praekelt mmoja wa wataalamu wa simu za viganjani wenye ufahamu mkubwa anasaidia kuendesha programu hiyo. ||| Gustav Praekelt one of the most knowledgeable mobile phone specialists in Africa is helping to run the program.
Mradi huo unafanywa kwa kutumia nafasi ya bure ya herufi au alama 120 katika mfumo wa jumbe za Tafadhali Nipigie Simuù unaotumika huko Afrika ya Kusini, wanaweka jumbe zitakazowafanya watu waende kutibiwa VVU kwa faragha, hivyo kutohofu doa au aibu inayoambatana na matibabu hayo. ||| It's done using the 120 character free space in Please Call Me SMS system thats used in South Africa. They tack on messages to get people to come to get HIV treatment in private, so that they don't have to worry about what stigma is attached to that treatment.ù
Doa au aibu, pamoja na taarifa potofu, vinaaminika kuwa ndiyo sababu kuu zinazosababisha Wa-Afrika ya Kusini wachache mno kujitokeza kutibiwa VVU. ||| Stigma, along with misinformation, are believed to be the main reasons why so few South Africans get tested and treated for HIV.
Japokuwa takriban watu wapatao milioni 5.7 nchini Afrika ya Kusini wanaishi na VVU, kwa mujibu wa waandalizi wa mradi huo ni asilimia 5 tu ya watu wamepimwa virusi hivyo. ||| Even though roughly 5.7 million people in South Africa are living with HIV, according to the project's organizers just 5 percent of the population has been tested for the virus.
Afrika ya Kusini pia ina idadi kubwa ya kesi za Kifua Kikuu, ugonjwa ambao unaua wengi wenye VVU. ||| South Africa also has one of the highest numbers of TB cases, a common killer of people with HIV.
Mradi M umeundwa ili kusaidia kupambana na magonjwa hayo mawili. ||| Project M was created to help combat both of these diseases.
3Sheep anaeleza kwamba utumiaji wa simu za viganjani unaofanywa na mradi huu unaonyesha ni jinsi gani simu hizo zimejikita katika utamaduni wa Afrika ya Kusini, na anaongeza: ||| 3Sheep points out that this project's use of cell phones shows how embedded they are in South African culture, adding:
Nchi nyingi hazina miundombinu inayotumia mtandao wa waya na zinaangalia mitandao ya simu za viganjani kama njia ya mawasiliano huko nyuma njia nyingine za mawasiliano kama vile redio, zingetumika kufanya kazi kama hii lakini mradi huu wa Afrika ya Kusini unaonyesha umuhimu wa kuziangalia njia zote ili kuufikia umma.ù ||| Many countries do not have an established hardwired infrastructure and are looking to the mobile network as means of mass communication Previously other media, such as radio, would have been used for such work but the South African project demonstrates the importance of considering all channels for outreach.ù
Japo huu sio mradi wa kwanza wa aina hii huko Afrika ya Kusini, waandaaji wanasema haya ni matumizi makubwa zaidi ya simu za viganjani yaliyowahi kujaribiwa ili kutuma taarifa za afya. ||| Though this is not the first of such projects in South Africa, organizers say it's the largest use ever of mobile phones for sending health information.
Na mpaka sasa mradi huo una matumaini makubwa. ||| And so far the project holds much promise.
Majaribio ya kwanza ya kampeni hii inayotumia ujumbe wa simu za viganjani ulisaidia kuongeza wastani mara tatu zaidi ya watu wanaopiga simu kwenye huduma ya simu ya UKIMWI mjini Johannersburg. ||| Early testing of this text messaging campaign helped triple the average daily call volume to the National AIDS Helpline in Johannesburg.
Kama mradi utafaulu baada ya kuzinduliwa, kunamatumaini kwamba mradi huu utaweza kusambazwa sehemu nyingine Afrika. ||| If the project is successful post-launch, it's hoped that this model can be expanded across Africa.
Akitoa maoni katika ujumbe uliotumwa kwenye African Globalization, ahellgeth, anaamini kwamba mradi huu una matumaini makubwa. ||| ahellgeth, commenting on a post on African Globalization, believes that this project has a lot of potential.
Utumiaji wa teknolojia ni njia nzuri ya kufikisha ujumbe wenye nguvu kwa umma. ||| Using technology is a great way to get a strong message across to a mass amount of people.
Utrumiaji wa ujumbe wa simu za viganjani unatoa fursa kwa watu kuusoma ujumbe mara kwa mara, ikilinganishwa kuangalia ujumbe kwenye matangazo ya biashara au mara moja tu kwenye vipeperushi. ||| The use of text messages offer people to view the message over and over, compared to seeing the message on a commercial or a flyer one time.
Ujumbe kwenye simu za viganjani hukaa kwenye simu kwa siku kadhaa, hii inamruhusu mtumiaji kurejea na kuangalia ujumbe huo. ||| A text message usually sits in a phone's mailbox for a couple of days, allowing that person to go back and view it.
Nadhani ujumbe utawafikia watu na kunasa na utawahamasisha kuchukua hatua jumbe hizi ni sawa na matangazo kwa ya wazi kwa umma kwa kutumia simu za viganjani.ù ||| I think the message would truly stick with people allowing them to act on it These texts are public service announcements for cell phones.ù
Akiblogu katika Design in Africa, Dave anaafiki kwamba mradi huu una uwezekano wa kufanikiwa: ||| Dave, blogging on Design in Africa agrees that this project will likely be a success:
Ni suala muhimu linalotatuliwa, ufumbuzi rahisi na unaoeleweka umebuniwa kwa kujumuisha hazina au nguvu za wadau, na kuna manufaa yanayopimika kwa watu na jamii na gharama za kupokea ujumbe bure. ||| An important issue is being addressed, a simple, easy to understand solution has been designed by combining the resources of stakeholders, there are measurable benefits for people and communities and the cost of the incoming message is free.
Akiblogu katika Wise Advice, lablady, anaona ni jambo linalosumbua kidogo kwamba teknolojia imwekwa kwenye ulingo mkuu katika vita dhidi ya VVU/UKIMWI. ||| But lablady, blogging on Wise Advice, finds it unsettling that technology has taken center-stage in the fight against HIV/AIDS.

Naliona hili ni jambo lililo kinyume, kwamba teknolojia sasa imekuwa ni chombo kinachoanzisha kampeni ambayo katika wakati mwingine, ingekuwa ni kampeni ya umma kwenye ngazi za chini kwenda kupima damu na kuelimishwa zaidi. ||| I find it paradoxical that technology has now become the default vehicle to initiate what would have been at one time, a grass roots blood testing and education campaign.
Je dharau kwa upande wangu kuhoji kwa nini umma mzima umiliki simu za mkononi kabla ya kunufaika na mkakati wa kinga ya afya kupingana na ugonjwa unaoweza kuzuilika?ù ||| Is it arrogant of me to wonder why an entire population acquired cell phones before they had access to a successful public health strategy for a preventable disease?ù
Naye Catherine Forsythe, akiblogu kwenye DogReader, anaongeza kwamba jumbe hizi hatimaye zitaweza kuchukuliwa kama jumbe za keroù za afya. ||| Catherine Forsythe, blogging on DogReader, adds that these messages may eventually be seen as health spam.ù
Swali linaweza kuwa òni kwa muda gani mbinu hii inaeweza kufanya kazi? Baada ya kusoma kwa mara ya kwanza, jumbe hizi za afya kwa umma zinaweza kufutwa mara moja kama vile zinavyofutwa jumbe nyingine za kero.ù ||| The question may be how long will this methodology be effective? After an initial viewing, these public health messages may be deleted as quickly as the usual text spam.ù
Ni matumaini ya Project M kwamba haitakuwa hivyo. ||| Project M certainly hopes not.
Awamu zijazo za mradi huu zitajumuisha usambazwaji wa vifaa vya kupimia VVU majumbani, pia uendelezwaji wa huduma za vituo vya simu mtandaoni,ù na utumiaji wa ujumbe wa maandishi wa simu za mkononi ili kutoa huduma binafsi za taarifa za afya kwa wale wanaotibiwa UKIMWI. ||| Future phases of the project involve distributing at-home HIV testing kits, developing virtual call centers,ù and using text messages to provide personalized healthcare information for those being treated for AIDS.

Mwanasheria anayeheshimika na mhadhiri kwenye Chuo Kikuu cha Ghana, Kitivo cha Sheria, Dr. Raymond Atuguba ameonyesha kwa umakini jinsi wanamgambo wa eneno la Delta ya Naija, wanaojulikana kwa ukorofi wa kulipua mabomba ya mafuta, kuteka watu nyara na kudai dhamana kubwa na kusababisha vurugu kwenye eneo lenye utajiri wa mafuta nchini Naijeria wameanza kuingia Ghana kwa makundi. ||| A respected legal practitioner and lecturer at the University of Ghana, Law Faculty, Dr. Raymond Atuguba has chillingly revealed that militants in the Niger Delta region, notorious for blowing up oil pipes, kidnapping and demanding huge ransoms and causing unrest in the oil rich Nigerian region have started tripping to Ghana in droves.

Profesa Abdelwahed, ambaye anafundisha Kiingereza Chuo Kikuu cha Al-Azhar anaandika katika Moments of Gaza: ||| Professor Said Abdelwahed, who teaches English at Al-Azhar University, writes at Moments of Gaza:
Leo yalikuwa mashambulizi ya nchi kavu. ||| Today was a ground offensive.
Raia wengi walifariki kwenye mashambulizi ya mabomu katika maeneo ya ukingoni mwa mji wa Gaza. ||| Many civilians died in the bombing of areas at the edges of Gaza city.
Umeme na maji bado ni matatizo makubwa kwa wakazi wote wa Gaza. ||| Electricity and water are still major problems for all Gazans.
Bado ninatumia jenereta kuweza kuandika jumbe hizi! ||| I am still operating a generator to be able to write those messages in minutes!
Simu za mikononi zimezimika na zile za majumbani zimeganda au hazisikiki vyema na wakati mwingine, husikika! ||| Mobile phones are paralyzed and land telephones are static or distorted and other times, it is clear!
Shambulio la anga karibu na hapa dakika chache zilizopita; hatujui lilitokea wapi lakini lilitisha. ||| An air raid nearby minutes back; we do not know where it was but it was so frightening.
Walipiga jengo lililo karibu! ||| They hit a nearby building!
Ni majengo matatu kutoka hapa nilipo; kuna majeruhi! ||| It's three building away from me; there are casualties!
Ndege za Israeli zinatupa mabomu ya radi au pengine ni miangaza inayotumiwa kwa madhumuni ya kijeshi. ||| Israeli aircrafts are throwing down lighting bombs or perhaps it they are lights for military purposes.
Israeli iliingilia idhaa ya setilaiti ya Al-Aqsa kwa mara kadhaa. ||| Israel intercepted Al-Aqsa satellite channel several times.
Walitangaza habari zinazoipinga Hamas. ||| They broadcasted anti-Hamas material.
Nitarejea tena kama nitaweza! ||| I will be back if could!

Tumesikia kuhusi vipeperushi ambavyo majeshi ya Israeli yanauchafua mji wa Gaza navyo wakiwaambia watu kuwa Hamas ndio wa kulaumiwa kwa matatizo yao, na sio ndege za kijeshi za F-16 na mabomu mengine. ||| We've heard about the flyers the Israeli army is littering Gaza with telling people Hamas is to blame for their woes, not their f-16s and cluster bombs.
Na hivi sasa wameanza kuwapigia watu simu kwa kutumia mashine za sauti kana kwamba ni Hilary Clinton, kwa muda wa masaa yote usiku na mchana. ||| Now, they have taken to robo-calling the citizens of Gaza a la Hilary Clinton, at all times of the night and day.
Baba yangu kapokea simu kadhaa pamoja na ile wakati tulipokwa tunamaliza mahojiano na CNN, tulikuwa tukitumia Skype. ||| My father has received a number of calls including one as we finished another CNN interview, and we were on skype.
Alijaribu kuiweka simu kwenye kipaza sauti ili nami niisikie. ||| He tried to put the phone on speaker for me.
Tafasiri ya haraka haraka ni kuwa: Ujumbe wa dharura: Onyo kwa raia wote wa Gaza. ||| The rough translations: urgent message: warning to the citizens of Gaza.
Hamas inawatumieni kama ngao. ||| Hamas is using you as human shields.
Msiwasikilize. ||| Do not listen to them.
Hamas wamewakimbia na wamejificha kwenye maficho yao. ||| Hamas has abandoned you and are hiding in their shelters.
Achaneni nao ù ||| Give up now ù
Aliweka simu chini kwa hasira, hakutaka kusikiliza ujumbe wote. ||| He hung up in disgust, not wanting to hear the rest.
Jeshi pia limekuwa likiwapigia simu watu kuwafahamisha kuwa nyumba zao zitashambuliwa. ||| The army has also been calling people to let them know their houses will be targeted.
Watu wameacha kupokea simu zao, na hawapokei simu zenye namba wasizozifahamu kutokana na kuogopa. ||| People have stopped answering their phones now, and do not take calls from unknown numbers from fear.
Sharon ni mwanaharakati anayeblogu katika blogu ya Tales to Tell, na kama wanaharakati wengine wa kimataifa mjini Gaza, anafanya awezalo ili kuwasaidia wafanyakazi wa afya wa dharura: ||| Sharon is an activist who blogs at Tales to Tell, and like many of the international activists in Gaza, is doing what she can to assist ambulance workers:
Tunashindwa kulipita shimo kubwa barabarani ambamo kuna gari lilikwishanasa ndani yake. ||| We are unable to pass a huge crater in the road into which a car has already nosedived.
Tulichukua njia ndefu ya mzunguko, tukamuokota mtu aliyevalia mavazi ya kitamaduni, wa makamo ndani ya miaka ya 60 hivi, kutoka katika linaloonekana ni shamba lake la ukoo. ||| Taking the long way round, we collect a man in traditional dress, in his 60s, from what seems to be his family farm.
Anatokwa damu usoni na mwenye hofu kubwa. ||| He is bleeding from the face and very frightened.
Njiani kuelekea hospitali ya Karmel Adwan mlipuko mmoja karibu kabisa na gari la wagonjwa ukalitetemesha gari. ||| On the way to Karmel Adwan hospital a particularly close explosion rocks the van.
Lazima nilishtuka kiasi, kwa sababu dereva aliniuliza je umesikia?ù ||| I must not have jumped enough, because the driver mimes did you hear that?ù to me.

4:55 Tunaondoka Al Shifa kurejea kwenye kituo cha Jabalia. ||| 10:55 We leave Al Shifa to head back to the Jabalia Centre.
Kuna kahawa. ||| There is coffee.
Mo anatengeza kahawa na mkate ambavyo si kawaida. ||| Mo makes a coffee sandwich, which is just weird.
Kuna ahueni kwenye idadi ya simu. ||| There is a pause in the calls.
Hassan ananiuliza kuhusu kitabu changu, Tiba Asiliaù; Ninamueleza kuwa ni kitabu kinachohusu safari ya mtaalamu wa mahusiano ya viumbe na mazingira kutoka kwenye ugonjwa wa mawazo. ||| Hassan asks me about my book, Nature Cureù; I explain it is about an ecologists route out of depression.
watu huugua ugonjwa wa mawazo kwenye nchi za magharibi?ù Aliuliza kwa mshangao. ||| People get depressed in the West?ù he asks in surprise.
Ninaelewa isivyoweza kuyumkinika kusikika hivi sasa, nasema watu wengi hujikuta wamejitega katika maisha ya kazi na ununuaji wa vitu tu, bila ya kuwa na maana katika maisha yao dini, au ndoto ya ukombozi wa nchi yako, au jambo kama hilo, watu wengi hupotea. ||| Understanding how implausible that must sound right now, I say that many people get caught up in a life that mainly holds work and buying stuff, and without some sort of meaning religion, or the dream of your land being free, or something like that, people can get very lost.
Kwa kweli Israeli inataka kutufanya tuwe hivyo hivi sasaù, alisema. ||| Actually Israel is trying to force us into a meaningless life like this,ù he says.
kwa mfano, saa nyingine jambo kubwa ambalo hulifikiria ni jinsi ya kupata kilo ya gesi, nilijenga jiko kwa ajili ya familia yangu na nilijisikia kana kwamba nilifanya jambo la kustaajabisha.ù ||| Like, sometimes I feel that all that really matters to me right now is a kilo of gas. I built a stove for my family and I feel like I did something amazing.ù
Katika ujumbe mwingine anatuambia: ||| In another post she tells us:
Tulimuuliza mtumishi wa mapokezi wa shirika la Hilali Nyekundu la Jabalia ni simu ngapi za dharura wanazozipokea kutoka sehemu ambazo Waisraeli hawawaruhusu kwenda. ||| We asked the Jabalia Red Crescent administrator person how much of the emergency calls Israel is not letting them go to.
Maeneo hayo ni yale ambayo uratibu wake lazima ufanywe na majeshi ya uvamizi kupitia shirika la Msalaba Mwekundu. ||| These are in areas where co-ordination must be made with the invading forces via the Red Cross to enter.
Alisema kuwa hawaruhusiwi kuhudumia asilimia takriban 80 ya simu zote zinazotokea kaskazini, amabpo ni sehemu za Beit Lahia, Beit Hanoun, na Jabalia. ||| He said they are not being allowed to attend to about 80 percent of the calls from the north, covering the Beit Lahia, Beit Hanoun, and Jabalia area.

Wanane kati ya watu kumi wanaoomba msaada huzuiliwa kupokea msaada huo. ||| Eight of ten people calling for help are being prevented from receiving it.
Mwanaharakati kutoka Kanada, Eva Bartlet, anblogu katika In Gaza: ||| Canadian activist, Eva Bartlett, blogs at In Gaza:
Idadi ya walioteketezwa na kujeruhiwa ni kubwa mno hivi sasa 521 na 3,000 kufikia asbuhi hii, kwa saa za Gaza kuketi pembeni ya maiti au mtu anayefariki inakuwa ni jambo la kawaida. ||| The numbers slaughtered and injured are so high now 521 and 3,000 as of this morning, Gaza time that sitting next to a dead or dying person is becoming normal.
Doa la damu kwenye machela ya gari la wagonjwa linasogeea karibu ya koti langu, na mganga ananionya kwamba koti langu linaweza kuchafuka. ||| The stain of blood on the ambulance stretcher pools next to my coat, the medic warning me my coat may be dirtied.
Kwani ninajali? Doa lile haliwezi kunikera kama ambavyo ningekereka, au ambavyo nilikereka wiki moja iliyopita. ||| The stain doesn't revolt me as it would have done, one week ago.
Mauti yamejaa hewani, kwenye mitaa ya Gaza, na siwezi kusisitiza zaidi kwamba siongei kwa kutia chumvi. ||| Death fills the air, the streets in Gaza, and I cannot stress that this is no exaggeration.
Nimerudi mjini Gaza kwa muda mchache, baada ya mchana na usiku wa kazi na wauguzi, nitajaribu kutoa muhtasari, ingawa kuna mengi ya kueleza, habari nyingi zinazojitokeza, na ni vigumu kuwafikia wananchi, hata wale walioko kilometa moja tu kutoka hapa. ||| Back in Gaza city briefly, after a day and night again with the medics, I'll try to summarize, though there is too much to tell, too much incoming news, and its too hard to reach people, even those just a kilometer away.
Kabla ya kunishusha wauguzi walikwenda kwenye vituo mbalimbali vya mafuta, wakitafuta mafuta kwa ajili ya gari la wagonjwa. ||| Before dropping me off, the medics had gone to different gas stations, searching for gas for the ambulances.
Walipita vituo viwili bila kubahatika. ||| Two stations, no luck.
Na wengine walipofika kwenye kituo cha mwisho walibahatika kujaza mafuta. ||| Some at a final source fills their tanks.
Uhaba wa mafuta umefikia hali mbaya. ||| The absence of gas is critical.
Kadhalika uhaba wa mikate, ambao unaendelea, na foleni ni ndefu kuliko. ||| So is the absence of bread, which goes on, the lines longer than ever yet.
Ujumbe wa maandishi kwenye simu ya mkononi unaniambia (katika kipindi hiki inanibidi nitegemee habari kutoka kwenye simu ya mkononi kama inawezekana kupokea) kwamba Umoja wa Mataifa unasema kuwa watu 13,000wamepoteza makazi yao, na kwamba asilimia 20 ya waliokufa ni wanawake na watoto, asilimia 70 hawana maji salama ya kunywa. ||| A text tells me (at this point I have to rely on news from phone and text messages, when reception is available) that the UN says 13,000 have been displaced since these attacks, that 20 percent of the dead are women and children, 70 percent are without drinking water.
Kuna taarifa nyingi zinazoweza kumlevya mtu na ugonjwa wa kutojali, lakini siwezi kuwaambia yote hivi sasa. ||| There are many more facts to sober one drunk on apathy, but I can't source or share them now.
Israeli imetuingilia majumbani, inapigana katika mitaa yetu na unaonyesha unyama wake dhidi kwa nguvu zote. ||| Israel has come into our homes, is fighting us in our streets and is expressing its brutality against us in full force.
Je tujibu vipi? ||| How do we react?
Makundi yote ya Wapalestinayameungana na yanampinga adui, kwa kutumia nguvu zao zote za kijeshi kwa pamoja. ||| All Palestinian factions have united and are out facing the enemy, using all the military capabilities that they collectively have.
Japokuwa nguvu hizohaziwezi kulingana na nguvu zilizoshinikizwa na Israeli, zimetufanya tuwe na hakika zaidi kwamba Wapalestina watapigana mpaka mwisho kulinda kile kilicho chao. ||| Although these capabilities are incomparable to the military strength exerted by Israel, yet it has made us more certain than ever that Palestinians will fight to the very end to protect their own.
Imetuonyesha kwamba mapambano ya upinzani, kujitoa muhanga na mapenzi ni sehemu ya Wapalestina ambayo haitaweza kubadilika pamoja na dhiki zote zinazotusibu. ||| It has shown us that resistance, courage and love are an integral part of the Palestinian identity that will never change despite all the hardships we endure.
Imetutia mwamko adili katika hisia zetu, mwamko ambao umetufikia katika wakati tunaouhitaji zaidi. ||| It has given us a moral boost, which comes at a time when we need it most.
Ni vigumu kukumbukawakati ambapo mahitaji ya msingi kama vile chakula, maji, vuguvugu la mapendo na mwanga wa juahavikuwa anasa. ||| It's hard even to remember a time when basic necessities such as food, water, warmth and daylight weren't a luxury.
Katika kipindi hiki ni haja za kibinaadamu opekee ambazo zinafanya kazi, haja ya kuwalinda wale uwapendao, haja ya kuhakikisha unayo malazi na maamuzi ya haraka ya aidha kukimbia au kupigana. ||| At this point, bare human instinct is at work, the need to protect your loved ones, the need to ensure shelter and the instinct of fight or flight.
Tumekuwa tukikimbia kwa muda mrefu sana, Gaza ndiyo kwetu na ndiyo ngome yetu ya mwisho baada ya kupoteza makazi yetu kule panapoitwa Israeli hivi sasa. ||| We have fled for too long, Gaza is our last refuge and our home after we were displaced from what is now called Israel.
Haya yote yalitokea miaka 60 tu iliyopita. ||| All this happened but 60 years ago.
Jingine lipi wanalolitaka? ||| What more could they want?
Hatuna pengine pa kwenda. ||| We have nowhere left to go.
Huu ndio wakati ambao kila mbinu ya upinzani ni ruksa kutumika. ||| Now is a time when all forms of resistance are legitimate.
Wamepuuza kila kila sheria ya kimataifa iliyopo. ||| They have disregarded every single international law there is.
Kwa hiyo huu ndio wakati wa kupigana. ||| So now is the time to fight.

Hakuna umeme hakuna mawasiliano ya simu kwenda nje. ||| No electricity no outgoing calls.
Giza na mvua ya moto inanyesha. ||| Darkness and it's raining fire.
Watoto wanapiga mayowe. ||| The children are screaming.
Mutasharrid (mtu asiye na makazi) yupo huko Khan Younis, na ana hasira: ||| Mutasharrid (homeless person or vagrant) is in Khan Younis, and is angry:
Niliulizwa jana kama misaada inafika Gaza au ni habari tu ya kwenye magazetiù. ||| I was asked yesterday whether the aid to Gaza was really getting in or if it was newspaper talkù.
Nilikataa kujibu kwani jawabu liko wazi, liko wazi kama ngurumo ya ndege za kijeshi za F-16 zinavyonguruma hivi sasa;usijali, misaada inayoingia Gaza, labda kwa kiwango kikubwa wakati wa siku zile za mwanzo, lakini ilisitishwa siku mbili zilizopita kwa madai ya operesheni ya kijeshi ya nchi kavu, hata hivyo, hilo halikubadili chochote! ||| I refused to respond because the answer is clear, as clear as the sound of F16 strike right now: never mind, the aid got into Gaza, maybe in great quantities in the first days, but stopped two days ago on the pretext of the ground operation, however, that did not count for much!
Yaani, ni vipi vyombo vya habari vimefanikiwa kuwasilisha shauri hili kama shauri moja la mtu mwenye njaa aliyezingirwa, anayetafuta misaada ya kibinaadamu na chakula kisichomfaa hata mbwa?! ||| I mean, how have the media succeeded in presenting the case of Gaza as one of a hungry person under siege, searching for food and humanitarianù aid not worthy of dogs?!
Nilipomuuliza raki yangu alinijibu Waarabu ni mfano wa watu wanaompiga mbwa huku wakimrushia mnofu wa nyama!ù ||| When I asked my friend he said, The Arabs are like a person firing on a dog and throwing it a piece of meat!ù
Gaza haitafuti aspirini kutibu jeraha lake, rafiki zangu, Gaza haitafuti bandeji kwa ajili kuziba mtiririko wa damu. ||| Gaza is not searching for an aspirin for its bloody wound, my friends, Gaza is not searching for a bandage for its continuous bleeding.
Kitu kinachoiumiza Gaza, na hasa kitu kinachoiua Gaza zaidi ya makombora ni sauti yake: sauti ya kila mtu anayevalia suti na tai anayeizungumzia Gaza. ||| What hurts Gaza, indeed kills it more than rockets, are their voices: the voice of every person wearing a suit and tie speaking about Gaza.
Utatatamani uwapayukie kwenye nyuso zao, kabla ya ndege, Nyamaza! ||| You wish you could scream in their faces, before the aircraft, Stop!
Sauti yako inajeruhi na ina makali zaidi ya ukimya wako, kwa hivyo kaa kimya Tuonee huruma, kaa kimya kwa kitambo kidogo ù ||| Your voice is wounding and is damned sharper than your silence, so stay silent Have mercy on us, stay silent a little while ù

Tuombeeni ||| Pray for us
Blogu yenye jina la Madhara kwa raia wakati wa mapambano mjini Gaza na Kusini mwa Israeli imetengenezwa na asaasi za haki za kibinaadamu za Kiisraeli ili kuorodhesha matukio ambayo hayaandikwi na vyombo vikubwa vya habari. ||| A blog called Harm to Civilians during the fighting in Gaza and Southern Israel has been set up by Israeli human rights groups to document events that are not being covered by the media.
Bolivia: Uhaba wa Maji Kwa Sababu ya Theluji Inayoyeyuka ||| Bolivia: Water Shortages Due to Melting Glaciers
Safu ya milima ya Chacaltaya ina baadhi ya vilele ambavyo ni alama zenye maana katika safu ya milima Andes iliyopo Bolivia. ||| The Chacaltaya mountain range contains some of the most symbolic peaks in Bolivia's Andes Mountains.
Kwa kuwa ilikuwa ni sehemu moja pekee ambapo mchezo wa kuteleza barafuni uliweza kufanyika katika nchi hii ya milimamilima, milima hii ni maarufu sana kwa wale walio kwenye Idara ya La Paz, na pia kwa wageni wapenda kuvumbua mambo mapya. ||| As it once was one of the only places to snow ski in this mountainous country, these mountains are well-known to those in the Department of La Paz, as well as foreign adventurers.
Ni katika milima hiyohiyo ambapo zilifanyika mechi za soka za hisani ambazo kwazo Rais Evo Morales alishiriki ili kuthibitisha kwamba michezo inaweza kuchezwa katika maeneo ya ukanda wa juu. ||| The mountains have also hosted charity football matches in which Bolivian President Evo Morales participated, seeking to prove that the sport can be played at high altitudes.
Hata hivyo, theluji ya Chacaltaya imeanza kupungua kwa kasi inayotisha na kali sana. ||| However, Chacaltaya's glacier has been receding at a worrisome and rapid pace.
Athari ya mabadiliko ya hali ya hewa kwa barafu iliyoko kwenye mlima huu na mingine iliyo katika eneo hili zimekuwa zikichunguzwa na Profesa wa Chuo Kikuu cha San Andras, Edson Rama≠rez, ambaye anahitimisha kwa kusema kwamba kuna uhusiano wa moja kwa moja kati ya kuongezeka kwa kiwango cha joto na kutokweka kwa theluji au barafu hiyo. ||| The effects of climate change on this glacier and others in the region have been part of the investigation by Higher University of San Andras professor Edson Rama≠rez, who concludes a direct connection between global warming and the disappearance of the glacier.
Rama≠rez na timu yake wamekuwa pia wakitafiti barafu iliyoko kwenye mlima mwingine ambao nao umekuwa ukipatwa na athari zinazofanana na huo mwingine na madhara ya mwenendo huo kwa jamii inayoishi maeneo ya jirani. ||| Rama≠rez and his team have also been studying another nearby glacier that is undergoing similar changes and about the effect on the local population.
barafu iliyoko kwenye mlima unaoitwa Tuni Condoriri glacier unayeyuka katika kasi kubwa, hivyo kuwaathiri wapenzi wa alpine, lakini pia hali hiyo inaathiri jamii za wahamiaji walio katika hatari ambao huitegemea ili kujipatia maji ya kunywa na kwa ajili ya shughuli za kilimo. ||| The Tuni Condoriri glacier is melting at a rapid pace, affecting alpine enthusiasts, but also affecting a vulnerable migrant population that depends on it for drinking water and agricultural activities.
Tenki la kuhifadhia maji yanayotoka kwenye barafu iliyoko kwenye mlima huo hutoa kiasi cha 80% cha maji ya kunywa kwa jiji la El Alto na vitongoji vyake vya La Paz. ||| The reservoir that collects the water from the glacier provides 80% of the drinking water to the city of El Alto and the outskirts of La Paz.
Kwa mujibu wa sensa ya hivi karibuni, El Alto ina jumla ya watu wapatao 827,000,ambapo idadi hiyo inakua kwa 5.1% kila mwaka. ||| According to the most recent census, El Alto has a population of 827,000 people, which is increasing every year at a rate of 5.1% per year.
Kwa mujibu wa mwandishi wa habari na mwanablogu Ma≥nica Oblitas, kiwango hiki ni zaidi ya mara mbili ya wastani wa taifa. ||| According to journalist and blogger Ma≥nica Oblitas, this rate is more than double the national average.
Wataalamu wanabashiri uhaba wa maji na kulipia maji, ambapo watu wengine wanabashiri kwamba suala la mgao wa maji limekaribia. ||| Experts are predicting water shortages and a premium for water, with some people predicting that water rationing is imminent.
Timu kutoka Wafuatiliaji wa Ulimwengu waliandaa makala ya video yenye sehemu sita kuonyesha madhara ya upungufu wa maji katika eneo hilo. ||| The team from Global Observer created a 6-part video series about the effects of future water shortages in this region.
Jiji hilo ni makazi ya wahamiaji kutoka jamii za wenyeji wa Aymara katika Altiplano ya Bolivia, ambao huhamia katika jiji la El Alto, mara nyingi wakiwa katika hali ya umaskini uliokithiri. ||| The city is home to migrants from the Aymara indigenous communities on the Bolivian Altiplano, who settle in El Alto, often in impoverished conditions.
Mwanablogu wa Ki-Bolivia, Cristina Quisbert anayeandika katika blogu ya Indigenous Bolivia anaelezea hali inayowakabili wakaazi wengi hususani kuhusu maji salama ya kunywa: ||| Bolivian blogger Cristina Quisbert of the blog Indigenous Bolivia describes the situation that many residents face in terms of suitable drinking water:
Kuna mambo mengine yanayochangia katika ugumu wa kupata maji. ||| Additional conditions difficult access to water.
Watu wengi wanafika kutoka vijijini kuingia katika jiji la El Alto na kuanzisha makazi pale wanapoweza kufanya hivyo. ||| A lot of people arrive from rural area to El Alto and establish wherever they can.
Kwa sababu ya ukosefu wa fedha, wanaishi popote pale mara nyingi ambapo hapana maji ya kunywa wala hakuna mfumo wa maji taka. ||| Because of lack of money, they live in neighborhoods where there is neither drinkable water nor sewer system.
Baadhi yao huchimba visima vifupi vya hadi mita tatu hivi hadi wapate maji. ||| Some of them dig a hole which should be about three metres deep until they find water.
Kwenye mwezi Novemba hivi, mvua za mwanzo huanza kunyesha, hivyo kufanya uwezekano wa kupata maji kwa majirani hawa. ||| More or less in November, it starts rainy time and it is other possibility for neighbors to collect water.
Mwishowe, uhaba wa maji huchangia katika kuongeza umaskini na vyote hivyo husababisha maradhi. ||| At the end, lack of water added to existent levels of poverty many times result in illnesses.
Kuna hali fulani ya mambo mbalimbali na tofauti kuwa pamoja. ||| There is an heterogeneity of situations.
Mimi napata maji nyumbani lakini jirani zangu hawapati. ||| I have water at home but some of my neighbors don't.
Hili ni jambo zito kwa familia. ||| This is a serious problem for the families.
Kwa upande wangu, ninawagawia maji familia nyingine. ||| In my case, I share water with other families.

Wanaishi katika nyumba ya kupanga. ||| They are renters.
Nyumba wanamoishi haina maji yanayofaa kunywa. ||| The house where they live doesn't have drinkable water.

mlima barafu wa Chacaltaya haupo tena, vilevile hivi karibuni milima barafu mingine nayo itatoweka. ||| Chacaltaya is no longer around and soon, other glaciers will cease to exist.
